  1604)    ! More pointers;  pbuf in convect_shallow.F90 (cam4) or stratiform.F90 (cam5)
  1605)    ! calc in hk_conv.F90 (CAM4 should be 0!), uwshcu.F90 but then affected by micro so values from stratiform.F90 (CAM5)
  1606)    real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: sh_cldliq   ! shallow gbm cloud liquid water (kg/kg)
  1607)    real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: sh_cldice   ! shallow gbm cloud ice water (kg/kg)
  1608)    ! More pointers;  pbuf in zm_conv_intr.F90, calc in zm_conv.F90, 0 for CAM4 and CAM5 (same convection scheme)
  1609)    real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: dp_cldliq   ! deep gbm cloud liquid water (kg/kg)
  1610)    real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: dp_cldice   ! deep gmb cloud ice water (kg/kg)
  1611) 
  1612)    !! precip mixing ratio pointers (could use for cam5?),  future if demanded to replace precip fluxes (##2do)
  1613)    ! More pointers;  added to pbuf in stratiform.F90, getting from pbuf here
  1614)    !real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: ls_mrprc       ! grid-box mean rain+snow mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  1615)    !real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: ls_mrsnw       ! grid-box mean snow mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  1616)    ! More pointers;  pbuf in ??, getting from pbuf here (i'm not sure how to do this...)
  1617)    !real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: sh_mrprc       ! grid-box mean rain+snow mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  1618)    !real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: sh_mrsnw       ! grid-box mean snow mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  1619)    ! More pointers;  pbuf in ??, getting from pbuf here (i'm not sure if this is possible...)
  1620)    !real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: dp_mrprc       ! grid-box mean rain+snow mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  1621)    !real(r8), pointer, dimension(:,:) :: dp_mrsnw       ! grid-box mean snow mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  1622) 
  1623)    ! Output CAM variables
  1624)    ! Notes:
  1625)    ! 1) use pcols (maximum number of columns that code could use, maybe 16)
  1626)    ! pcols vs. ncol.  ncol is the number of columns a chunk is actually using, pcols is maximum number
  1627)    ! 2) Mixed variables rules/notes, need to collapse because CAM history does not support increased dimensionality
  1628)    ! MIXED DIMS: ntau_cosp*nprs_cosp, ndbze_cosp*nht_cosp, nsr_cosp*nht_cosp, nscol_cosp*nhtml_cosp, ntau_cosp*nhtmisr_cosp
  1629)    !    a) always making mixed variables VERTICAL*OTHER, e.g., pressure*tau or ht*dbze
  1630)    !    b) always collapsing output as V1_1/V2_1...V1_1/V2_N ; V1_2/V2_1 ...V1_2/V2_N etc. to V1_N/V2_1 ... V1_N/V2_N
  1631)    !    c) here, need vars for both multi-dimensional output from COSP, and two-dimensional output from CAM
  1632)    ! 3) ntime=1, nprofile=ncol
  1633)    ! 4) dimensions listed in COSP units are from netcdf output from cosp test case, and are not necessarily in the 
  1634)    !    correct order.  In fact, most of them are not as I discovered after trying to run COSP in-line.
  1635)    !    BE says this could be because FORTRAN and C (netcdf defaults to C) have different conventions.
  1636)    ! 5) !! Note: after running COSP, it looks like height_mlev is actually the model levels after all!!
  1637) 
  1638)    real(r8) :: clisccp2(pcols,ntau_cosp,nprs_cosp)      ! clisccp2 (time,tau,plev,profile)
  1639)    real(r8) :: cfad_dbze94(pcols,ndbze_cosp,nht_cosp)   ! cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile)
  1640)    real(r8) :: cfad_lidarsr532(pcols,nsr_cosp,nht_cosp) ! cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  1641)    real(r8) :: dbze94(pcols,nscol_cosp,nhtml_cosp)      ! dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  1642)    real(r8) :: atb532(pcols,nscol_cosp,nhtml_cosp)      ! atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  1643)    real(r8) :: clMISR(pcols,ntau_cosp,nhtmisr_cosp)     ! clMISR (time,tau,CTH_height_bin,profile)
  1644)    real(r8) :: frac_out(pcols,nscol_cosp,nhtml_cosp)    ! frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  1645)    real(r8) :: cldtot_isccp(pcols)                      ! CAM tclisccp (time,profile)
  1646)    real(r8) :: meancldalb_isccp(pcols)                  ! CAM albisccp (time,profile)
  1647)    real(r8) :: meanptop_isccp(pcols)                    ! CAM ctpisccp (time,profile)
  1648)    real(r8) :: cldlow_cal(pcols)                        ! CAM cllcalipso (time,profile)
  1649)    real(r8) :: cldmed_cal(pcols)                        ! CAM clmcalipso (time,profile)
  1650)    real(r8) :: cldhgh_cal(pcols)                        ! CAM clhcalipso (time,profile)
  1651)    real(r8) :: cldtot_cal(pcols)                        ! CAM cltcalipso (time,profile)
  1652)    real(r8) :: cld_cal(pcols,nht_cosp)                  ! CAM clcalipso (time,height,profile)
  1653)    real(r8) :: cfad_dbze94_cs(pcols,nht_cosp*ndbze_cosp)! CAM cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile)
  1654)    real(r8) :: cfad_sr532_cal(pcols,nht_cosp*nsr_cosp)  ! CAM cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  1655)    real(r8) :: tau_isccp(pcols,nscol_cosp)              ! CAM boxtauisccp (time,column,profile)
  1656)    real(r8) :: cldptop_isccp(pcols,nscol_cosp)          ! CAM boxptopisccp (time,column,profile)
  1657)    real(r8) :: meantau_isccp(pcols)                     ! CAM tauisccp (time,profile)
  1658)    real(r8) :: meantb_isccp(pcols)                      ! CAM meantbisccp (time,profile)
  1659)    real(r8) :: meantbclr_isccp(pcols)                   ! CAM meantbclrisccp (time,profile)     
  1660)    real(r8) :: dbze_cs(pcols,nhtml_cosp*nscol_cosp)     ! CAM dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  1661)    real(r8) :: cldtot_calcs(pcols)                      ! CAM cltlidarradar (time,profile)
  1662)    real(r8) :: cldtot_cs(pcols)                         ! CAM cltradar (time,profile)
  1663)    real(r8) :: cldtot_cs2(pcols)                        ! CAM cltradar2 (time,profile)
  1664)    real(r8) :: cld_cal_notcs(pcols,nht_cosp)            ! CAM clcalipso2 (time,height,profile)
  1665)    real(r8) :: atb532_cal(pcols,nhtml_cosp*nscol_cosp)  ! CAM atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  1666)    real(r8) :: mol532_cal(pcols,nhtml_cosp)             ! CAM beta_mol532 (time,height_mlev,profile)
  1667)    real(r8) :: cld_misr(pcols,nhtmisr_cosp*ntau_cosp)   ! CAM clMISR (time,tau,CTH_height_bin,profile)
  1668)    real(r8) :: refl_parasol(pcols,nsza_cosp)            ! CAM parasol_refl (time,sza,profile)
  1669)    real(r8) :: scops_out(pcols,nhtml_cosp*nscol_cosp)   ! CAM frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  1670)    real(r8) :: cltmodis(pcols)
  1671)    real(r8) :: clwmodis(pcols)
  1672)    real(r8) :: climodis(pcols)
  1673)    real(r8) :: clhmodis(pcols)
  1674)    real(r8) :: clmmodis(pcols)
  1675)    real(r8) :: cllmodis(pcols)
  1676)    real(r8) :: tautmodis(pcols)
  1677)    real(r8) :: tauwmodis(pcols)
  1678)    real(r8) :: tauimodis(pcols)
  1679)    real(r8) :: tautlogmodis(pcols)
  1680)    real(r8) :: tauwlogmodis(pcols)
  1681)    real(r8) :: tauilogmodis(pcols)
  1682)    real(r8) :: reffclwmodis(pcols)
  1683)    real(r8) :: reffclimodis(pcols)
  1684)    real(r8) :: pctmodis(pcols)
  1685)    real(r8) :: lwpmodis(pcols)
  1686)    real(r8) :: iwpmodis(pcols)
  1687)    real(r8) :: clmodis_cam(pcols,ntau_cosp_modis*nprs_cosp)
  1688)    real(r8) :: clmodis(pcols,ntau_cosp_modis,nprs_cosp)
  1689) 
  1690)    type(interp_type)  :: interp_wgts
  1691)    integer, parameter :: extrap_method = 1              ! sets extrapolation method to boundary value (1)
  1692) 
  1693)   !---------------- End of declaration of variables --------------
  1694) 
  1695)    !! find the chunk and ncol from the state vector
  1696)    lchnk = state%lchnk   !! state variable contains a number of columns, one chunk
  1697)    ncol = state%ncol     !! number of columns in the chunk
  1698) 
  1699)    ! initialize temporary variables as R_UNDEF - need to do this otherwise array expansion puts garbage in history
  1700)    ! file for columns over which COSP did make calculations.
  1701)    tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1702)    tmp1(1:pcols,1:pver)=R_UNDEF
  1703)    tmp2(1:pcols,1:pver)=R_UNDEF
  1704) 
  1705)    ! Initialize CAM variables as R_UNDEF, important for history files because it will exclude these from averages
  1706)    ! (multi-dimensional output that will be collapsed)
  1707)    ! initialize over all pcols, not just ncol.  missing values needed in chunks where ncol<pcols
  1708)    clisccp2(1:pcols,1:ntau_cosp,1:nprs_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1709)    cfad_dbze94(1:pcols,1:ndbze_cosp,1:nht_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1710)    cfad_lidarsr532(1:pcols,1:nsr_cosp,1:nht_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1711)    dbze94(1:pcols,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1712)    atb532(1:pcols,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1713)    clMISR(1:pcols,ntau_cosp,1:nhtmisr_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1714)    frac_out(1:pcols,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1715) 
  1716)    ! (all CAM output variables. including collapsed variables)
  1717)    cldtot_isccp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1718)    meancldalb_isccp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1719)    meanptop_isccp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1720)    cldlow_cal(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1721)    cldmed_cal(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1722)    cldhgh_cal(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1723)    cldtot_cal(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1724)    cld_cal(1:pcols,1:nht_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1725)    cfad_dbze94_cs(1:pcols,1:nht_cosp*ndbze_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1726)    cfad_sr532_cal(1:pcols,1:nht_cosp*nsr_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1727)    tau_isccp(1:pcols,1:nscol_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1728)    cldptop_isccp(1:pcols,1:nscol_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1729)    meantau_isccp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1730)    meantb_isccp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1731)    meantbclr_isccp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF     
  1732)    dbze_cs(1:pcols,1:nhtml_cosp*nscol_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1733)    cldtot_calcs(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1734)    cldtot_cs(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1735)    cldtot_cs2(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1736)    cld_cal_notcs(1:pcols,1:nht_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1737)    atb532_cal(1:pcols,1:nhtml_cosp*nscol_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1738)    mol532_cal(1:pcols,1:nhtml_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1739)    cld_misr(1:pcols,1:nhtmisr_cosp*ntau_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1740)    refl_parasol(1:pcols,1:nsza_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1741)    scops_out(1:pcols,1:nhtml_cosp*nscol_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1742)    cltmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1743)    clwmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1744)    climodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1745)    clhmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1746)    clmmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1747)    cllmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1748)    tautmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1749)    tauwmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1750)    tauimodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1751)    tautlogmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1752)    tauwlogmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1753)    tauilogmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1754)    reffclwmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1755)    reffclimodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1756)    pctmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1757)    lwpmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1758)    iwpmodis(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  1759)    clmodis_cam(1:pcols,1:ntau_cosp_modis*nprs_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1760)    clmodis(1:pcols,1:ntau_cosp_modis,1:nprs_cosp)=R_UNDEF
  1761) 
  1762) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  1763) ! DECIDE WHICH COLUMNS YOU ARE GOING TO RUN COSP ON....
  1764) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  1765) 
  1766) !! run_cosp is set for each column in each chunk in the first timestep of the run
  1767) !! hist_fld_col_active in cam_history.F90 is used to decide if you need to run cosp.
  1768) 
  1769) if (first_run_cosp(lchnk)) then
  1770) 
  1771)    !! initalize to run logicals as false
  1772)    run_cosp(1:ncol,lchnk)=.false.
  1773)    run_radar(1:nf_radar,1:ncol)=.false.
  1774)    run_lidar(1:nf_lidar,1:ncol)=.false.
  1775)    run_isccp(1:nf_isccp,1:ncol)=.false.
  1776)    run_misr(1:nf_misr,1:ncol)=.false.
  1777)    run_modis(1:nf_modis,1:ncol)=.false.
  1778) 
  1779)    if (lradar_sim) then
  1780)      do i=1,nf_radar
  1781)         run_radar(i,1:pcols)=hist_fld_col_active(fname_radar(i),lchnk)
  1782)      end do
  1783)    end if
  1784)    if (llidar_sim) then
  1785)      do i=1,nf_lidar
  1786)         run_lidar(i,1:pcols)=hist_fld_col_active(fname_lidar(i),lchnk)
  1787)      end do
  1788)    end if
  1789)    if (lisccp_sim) then
  1790)      do i=1,nf_isccp
  1791)         run_isccp(i,1:pcols)=hist_fld_col_active(fname_isccp(i),lchnk)
  1792)      end do
  1793)    end if
  1794)    if (lmisr_sim) then
  1795)      do i=1,nf_misr
  1796)         run_misr(i,1:pcols)=hist_fld_col_active(fname_misr(i),lchnk)
  1797)      end do
  1798)    end if
  1799)    if (lmodis_sim) then
  1800)      do i=1,nf_modis
  1801)         run_modis(i,1:pcols)=hist_fld_col_active(fname_modis(i),lchnk)
  1802)      end do
  1803)    end if
  1804) 
  1805)    do i=1,ncol
  1806)      if ((any(run_radar(:,i))) .or. (any(run_lidar(:,i))) .or. (any(run_isccp(:,i))) &
  1807)                 .or. (any(run_misr(:,i))) .or. (any(run_modis(:,i)))) then
  1808)         run_cosp(i,lchnk)=.true.
  1809)      end if
  1810)    end do
  1811) 
  1812)    first_run_cosp(lchnk)=.false.
  1813) 
  1814)    !!print *, first_run_cosp
  1815)    !!print *, run_cosp(1:ncol,lchnk)
  1816)    !!if (any(first_run_cosp)) then
  1817)    !!else
  1818)    !!print *, 'done'
  1819)    !!print *, run_cosp
  1820)    !!end if
  1821) 
  1822) end if
  1823) 
  1824) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  1825) ! POPULATE COSP CONFIGURATION INPUT VARIABLE ("cfg") FROM CAM NAMELIST
  1826) ! Note: This is a first cut, and these values may get overwritten later.
  1827) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  1828) 
  1829) ! Define/assign settings that would otherwise be read in using the COSP namelist.
  1830) ! (e.g., used cosp_test.f90 to identify necessary inputs to COSP and run structure)
  1831) 
  1832) ! SET COSP RUN OPTIONS
  1833) ! values come from namelist within atm_in namelist read in by cospsimulator_intr_readnl
  1834) ! note: some of these will be changed depending on the namelist variables later
  1835) 
  1836)    !print *, 'Populating cfg for COSP...'
  1837)    !!! checked cfg% structure vs. cosp_types.f90 v1.3
  1838) 
  1839)    ! Simulator flags
  1840)    cfg%Lradar_sim=lradar_sim
  1841)    cfg%Llidar_sim=llidar_sim
  1842)    cfg%Lisccp_sim=lisccp_sim
  1843)    cfg%Lmisr_sim=lmisr_sim
  1844)    cfg%Lmodis_sim=lmodis_sim
  1845)    cfg%Lrttov_sim=lrttov_sim
  1846)    cfg%Lalbisccp=lalbisccp
  1847)    cfg%Latb532=latb532

  1851)    cfg%LcfadLidarsr532=lcfad_lidarsr532
  1852)    cfg%Lclcalipso=lclcalipso
  1853)    cfg%Lclhcalipso=lclhcalipso
  1854)    cfg%Lclisccp=lclisccp2
  1855)    cfg%Lcllcalipso=lcllcalipso

  1857)    cfg%Lcltcalipso=lcltcalipso

  1859)    cfg%Ldbze94=ldbze94
  1860)    cfg%Lcltradar=lcltradar
  1861)    cfg%Lcltradar2=lcltradar2

  1864)    cfg%Llongitude=llongitude
  1865)    cfg%Llatitude=llatitude
  1866)    cfg%LparasolRefl=lparasol_refl
  1867)    cfg%LclMISR=lclMISR
  1868)    cfg%Lmeantbisccp=lmeantbisccp

  1870)    cfg%Lclcalipso2=lclcalipso2
  1871)    cfg%Lcltlidarradar=lcltlidarradar
  1872)    cfg%Lfracout=lfrac_out
  1873)    cfg%LlidarBetaMol532=lbeta_mol532
  1874)    cfg%Lcltmodis=lcltmodis
  1875)    cfg%Lclwmodis=lclwmodis
  1876)    cfg%Lclimodis=lclimodis
  1877)    cfg%Lclhmodis=lclhmodis
  1878)    cfg%Lclmmodis=lclmmodis
  1879)    cfg%Lcllmodis=lcllmodis
  1880)    cfg%Ltautmodis=ltautmodis
  1881)    cfg%Ltauwmodis=ltauwmodis
  1882)    cfg%Ltauimodis=ltauimodis
  1883)    cfg%Ltautlogmodis=ltautlogmodis
  1884)    cfg%Ltauwlogmodis=ltauwlogmodis
  1885)    cfg%Ltauilogmodis=ltauilogmodis
  1886)    cfg%Lreffclwmodis=lreffclwmodis
  1887)    cfg%Lreffclimodis=lreffclimodis
  1888)    cfg%Lpctmodis=lpctmodis
  1889)    cfg%Llwpmodis=llwpmodis
  1890)    cfg%Liwpmodis=liwpmodis
  1891)    cfg%Lclmodis=lclmodis
  1892)    cfg%Ltbrttov=ltbrttov
  1893) 
  1894)    ! make COSP radar and lidar stats are calculated
  1895)    ! from line 1464 of cosp_io.f90 (cosp_io.f90 code not included here, so need specify this cfg% option)
  1896)    if ((Lradar_sim).or.(Llidar_sim).or.(Lisccp_sim)) cfg%Lstats = .true.
  1897) 
  1898)    cfg%Lwrite_output=.false.  !! COSP I/O not used, should always be .false.
  1899) 
  1900) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  1901) ! GET CAM GEOPHYSICAL VARIABLES NEEDED FOR COSP INPUT
  1902) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  1903) 
  1904) ! 1) state variables (prognostic variables, see physics_types.F90)
  1905) ! state vars are passed to this subroutine from radiation.F90.   
  1906) ! I do not need to define these variables.  I can use them as is, e.g., state%t
  1907)    !state%lat   ! lat (radians) 
  1908)    !state%lon   ! lon (radians) 
  1909)    !state%t     ! temperature (K)
  1910)    !state%u     ! u_wind zonal wind (m/s)
  1911)    !state%v     ! v_wind meridional wind (m/s)
  1912)    !state%ps    ! surface pressure (Pa)
  1913)    !state%pint  ! p - p_in_full_levels (Pa)
  1914)    !state%pmid  ! ph - p_in_half_levels (Pa)
  1915)    !state%zm    ! geopotential height above surface at midpoints (m), pver
  1916)    !state%zi    ! geopotential height above surface at interfaces (m), pverp
  1917)    !state%phis  ! surface geopotential (m2/s2)
  1918)    ! NOTE: The state variables state%q(:,:,ixcldliq)/state%q(:,:,ixcldice) are grid-box
  1919)    ! quantities for the stratiform clouds only.  stratiform water * stratiform cloud fraction
  1920)    !state%q(:,:,ixcldliq) !for CAM4: cldliq= stratiform incld water content * total cloud fraction
  1921)    !state%q(:,:,ixcldice) !for CAM4: cldice = stratiform incld ice content * total cloud fraction
  1922) 
  1923)    ! need query index for cldliq and cldice
  1924)    ! use cnst_get_ind subroutine in constituents.F90.
  1925)    ! can also get MG microphysics number from state using similar procedure.
  1926)    call cnst_get_ind('CLDLIQ',ixcldliq)  !! replaced cnst_names(1) not setting abort flag which is optional in cnst_get_ind
  1927)    call cnst_get_ind(cnst_names(2),ixcldice)
  1928) 
  1929)    Npoints = ncol        ! default is running all columns in the chunk, not pcols = maximum number
  1930)    Nlevels = pver
  1931) 
  1932) ! 2) cam_in variables (see camsrfexch.F90)
  1933) ! I can reference these as is, e.g., cam_in%ts.  
  1934)    !cam_in%ts                   ! skt - Skin temperature (K)
  1935)    !cam_in%landfrac             ! land fraction, used to define a landmask (0 or 1) for COSP input
  1936) 
  1937) ! 3) radiative constituent interface variables:
  1938) ! specific humidity (q), 03, CH4,C02, N20 mass mixing ratio
  1939) ! Note: these all have dims (pcol,pver) but the values don't change much for the well-mixed gases.
  1940)     call rad_cnst_get_gas(0,'H2O', state, pbuf,  q)                     
  1941)     call rad_cnst_get_gas(0,'O3',  state, pbuf,  o3)
  1942)     call rad_cnst_get_gas(0,'CH4', state, pbuf,  ch4)
  1943)     call rad_cnst_get_gas(0,'CO2', state, pbuf,  co2)
  1944)     call rad_cnst_get_gas(0,'N2O', state, pbuf,  n2o)
  1945) 
  1946) ! 4) get variables from physics buffer
  1947)    itim_old = pbuf_old_tim_idx()
  1948) 
  1949)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, cld_idx,    cld,    start=(/1,1,itim_old/), kount=(/pcols,pver,1/) )
  1950)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, concld_idx, concld, start=(/1,1,itim_old/), kount=(/pcols,pver,1/) )
  1951) 
  1952)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, rel_idx, rel  )
  1953) 
  1954)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, rei_idx, rei)
  1955) 
  1956) !added some more sizes to physics buffer in stratiform.F90 for COSP inputs
  1957)    if( cam_physpkg_is('cam5') ) then
  1958)      call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, lsreffrain_idx, ls_reffrain  )
  1959)      call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, lsreffsnow_idx, ls_reffsnow  )
  1960)      call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, cvreffliq_idx,  cv_reffliq   )
  1961)      call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, cvreffice_idx,  cv_reffice   )
  1962)    end if
  1963) 
  1964)    ! Variables I added to physics buffer in other interfaces (not radiation.F90)
  1965)    ! all "1" at the end ok as is because radiation/intr after when these were added to physics buffer
  1966) 
  1967)    !!! convective cloud mixing ratios (use for cam4 and cam5)
  1968) 
  1969)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, dpcldliq_idx, dp_cldliq  )
  1970)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, dpcldice_idx, dp_cldice  )
  1971)    if( cam_physpkg_is('cam3') .or. cam_physpkg_is('cam4') ) then
  1972)       !!! get from pbuf in convect_shallow.F90
  1973)       call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, shcldliq_idx, sh_cldliq  )
  1974)       call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, shcldice_idx, sh_cldice  )
  1975)    elseif( cam_physpkg_is('cam5') ) then
  1976)       !!! get from pbuf in stratiform.F90
  1977)       call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, shcldliq1_idx, sh_cldliq  )
  1978)       call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, shcldice1_idx, sh_cldice  )
  1979)    end if
  1980) 
  1981)    !!! precipitation fluxes (use for both cam4 and cam5 for now....)
  1982)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, dpflxprc_idx, dp_flxprc  )
  1983)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, dpflxsnw_idx, dp_flxsnw  )
  1984)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, shflxprc_idx, sh_flxprc  )
  1985)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, shflxsnw_idx, sh_flxsnw  )
  1986)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, lsflxprc_idx, ls_flxprc  )
  1987)    call pbuf_get_field(pbuf, lsflxsnw_idx, ls_flxsnw  )
  1988) 
  1989) !!! precipitation mixing ratios (NOT WORKING, LEAVE COMMENTED OUT)
  1990) !   if ( CAM5 ) then
  1991)         !!! large-scale total and snow mixing ratios
  1992)         !!! exist as local fields in stratiform_tend subsroutine in stratiform.F90 (will become microp_driver_tend.F90)
  1993)         !ifld = pbuf_get_fld_idx('LS_MRPRC')
  1994)         !ls_mrprc  => pbuf(ifld)%fld_ptr(1,1:pcols,1:pver,lchnk, 1)
  1995)         !ifld = pbuf_get_fld_idx('LS_MRSNW')
  1996)         !ls_mrsnw  => pbuf(ifld)%fld_ptr(1,1:pcols,1:pver,lchnk, 1)
  1997)         !!! shallow convective total and snow mixing ratios (NOT IN PHYSICS BUFFER)
  1998)         !ifld = pbuf_get_fld_idx('SH_MRPRC')
  1999)         !sh_mrprc  => pbuf(ifld)%fld_ptr(1,1:pcols,1:pver,lchnk, 1)
  2000)         !ifld = pbuf_get_fld_idx('SH_MRSNW')
  2001)         !sh_mrsnw  => pbuf(ifld)%fld_ptr(1,1:pcols,1:pver,lchnk, 1)
  2002)         !!! deep convective total and snow mixing ratios (NOT IN PHYSICS BUFFER)
  2003)         !ifld = pbuf_get_fld_idx('DP_MRPRC')
  2004)         !dp_mrprc  => pbuf(ifld)%fld_ptr(1,1:pcols,1:pver,lchnk, 1)
  2005)         !ifld = pbuf_get_fld_idx('DP_MRSNW')
  2006)         !dp_mrsnw  => pbuf(ifld)%fld_ptr(1,1:pcols,1:pver,lchnk, 1)
  2007) !   end if
  2008) 
  2009) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2010) ! CALCULATE COSP INPUT VARIABLES FROM CAM VARIABLES, done for all columns within chunk
  2011) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2012) 
  2013) ! 0)create ptop/ztop for gbx%pf and gbx%zlev are for the the interface, 
  2014) !  also reverse CAM height/pressure values for input into CSOP
  2015) !  CAM state%pint from top to surface, COSP wants surface to top.
  2016) 
  2017)    ! initalize
  2018)    ptop(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2019)    pbot(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2020)    ztop(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2021)    zbot(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2022)    zmid(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2023) 
  2024)    ! assign values from top   
  2025)    do k=1,pverp-1
  2026)         ! assign values from top
  2027)         ptop(1:ncol,k)=state%pint(1:ncol,pverp-k)
  2028)         ztop(1:ncol,k)=state%zi(1:ncol,pverp-k)
  2029)         ! assign values from bottom           
  2030)         pbot(1:ncol,k)=state%pint(1:ncol,pverp-k+1)
  2031)         zbot(1:ncol,k)=state%zi(1:ncol,pverp-k+1)
  2032)    end do
  2033) 
  2034) 
  2035)    ! add surface height (surface geopotential/gravity) to convert CAM heights based on geopotential above surface into height above sea level
  2036)    do k=1,pver
  2037)    do i=1,ncol
  2038)      ztop(i,k)=ztop(i,k)+state%phis(i)/gravit  
  2039)      zbot(i,k)=zbot(i,k)+state%phis(i)/gravit
  2040)      zmid(i,k)=state%zm(i,k)+state%phis(i)/gravit
  2041)    end do    
  2042)    end do
  2043) 
  2044) ! 1) lat/lon - convert from radians to cosp input type
  2045) 
  2046)    ! initalize lat and lons
  2047)    lat_cosp(1:ncol)=0._r8
  2048)    lon_cosp(1:ncol)=0._r8
  2049)    ! convert from radians to degrees_north and degrees_east 
  2050)    lat_cosp=state%lat*180._r8/(pi)  ! needs to go from -90 to +90 degrees north
  2051)    lon_cosp=state%lon*180._r8/(pi)  ! needs to go from 0 to 360 degrees east
  2052) 
  2053) ! 2) rh - relative_humidity_liquid_water (%)
  2054) 
  2055)    ! calculate from CAM q and t using CAM built-in functions
  2056)    call qsat_water(state%t(1:ncol,1:pver), state%pmid(1:ncol,1:pver), &
  2057)         es(1:ncol,1:pver), qs(1:ncol,1:pver))
  2058) 
  2059)    ! initialize rh
  2060)    rh(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2061) 
  2062)    ! calculate rh
  2063)    do k=1,pver
  2064)    do i=1,ncol
  2065)         rh(i,k)=(q(i,k)/qs(i,k))*100
  2066)    end do
  2067)    end do
  2068) 
  2069) ! 3) landmask - calculate from cam_in%landfrac
  2070) 
  2071)    ! initalize landmask
  2072)    landmask(1:ncol)=0._r8
  2073)    ! calculate landmask
  2074)    do i=1,ncol
  2075)         if (cam_in%landfrac(i).gt.0.01_r8) landmask(i)= 1
  2076)    end do
  2077) 
  2078) ! 4) calculate necessary input cloud/precip variables
  2079) ! CAM4 note: don't take the cloud water from the hack shallow convection scheme or the deep convection.  
  2080) ! cloud water values for convection are the same as the stratiform value. (Sungsu)
  2081) ! all precip fluxes are mid points, all values are grid-box mean ("gbm") (Yuying)
  2082) 
  2083)    ! initialize local variables
  2084)    mr_ccliq(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2085)    mr_ccice(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2086)    mr_lsliq(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2087)    mr_lsice(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2088)    grpl_ls_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2089)    rain_ls_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8 
  2090)    snow_ls_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2091)    rain_cv(1:ncol,1:pverp)=0._r8
  2092)    snow_cv(1:ncol,1:pverp)=0._r8
  2093)    rain_cv_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2094)    snow_cv_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)=0._r8
  2095) 
  2096)    reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,1:nhydro)=0._r8
  2097)    ! note: reff_cosp dimensions should be same as cosp (reff_cosp has 9 hydrometeor dimension)
  2098)    ! Reff(Npoints,Nlevels,N_HYDRO)
  2099) 
  2100)    if( cam_physpkg_is('cam3') .or. cam_physpkg_is('cam4') ) then
  2101) 
  2102)       ! CAM4 settings, using precipitation fluxes as COSP inputs
  2103)       use_precipitation_fluxes = .true.
  2104) 
  2105)       ! add together deep and shallow convection precipitation fluxes, recall *_flxprc variables are rain+snow
  2106)       rain_cv(1:ncol,1:pverp) = (sh_flxprc(1:ncol,1:pverp)-sh_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp)) + &
  2107)                                 (dp_flxprc(1:ncol,1:pverp)-dp_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp))
  2108)       snow_cv(1:ncol,1:pverp) = sh_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp) + dp_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp)
  2109) 
  2110)       ! interpolate interface precip fluxes to mid points
  2111)       ! rain_cv_interp (pver) from rain_cv (pverp), snow_cv_interp from snow_cv, 
  2112)       ! rain_ls_interp from ls_flxprc-ls_flxsnw, snow_ls_interp from ls_flxsnw
  2113)       ! interpolate, loop over columns (can also put ":" but this gives less information)
  2114)       ! use interpolate_data.F90 in atm/cam/src/control
  2115)       do i=1,ncol
  2116)               ! find weights (pressure weighting?)
  2117)               call lininterp_init(state%zi(i,1:pverp),pverp,state%zm(i,1:pver),pver,extrap_method,interp_wgts)
  2118)               ! interpolate  lininterp1d(arrin, nin, arrout, nout, interp_wgts)
  2119)               ! note: lininterp is an interface, contains lininterp1d -- code figures out to use lininterp1d.
  2120)               call lininterp(rain_cv(i,1:pverp),pverp,rain_cv_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2121)               call lininterp(snow_cv(i,1:pverp),pverp,snow_cv_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2122)               call lininterp(ls_flxprc(i,1:pverp),pverp,rain_ls_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2123)               call lininterp(ls_flxsnw(i,1:pverp),pverp,snow_ls_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2124)               call lininterp_finish(interp_wgts)
  2125)               !! ls_flxprc is for rain+snow, find rain_ls_interp by subtracting off snow_ls_interp
  2126)               rain_ls_interp(i,1:pver)=rain_ls_interp(i,1:pver)-snow_ls_interp(i,1:pver)
  2127)       end do
  2128) 
  2129)       !! CAM4 mixing ratio calculations
  2130)       do k=1,pver
  2131)       do i=1,ncol
  2132)            if (cld(i,k) .gt. 0._r8) then
  2133)               !! note: cld and grid-box cloud water contents in state vector includes both the stratiform and the convective cloud fractions.
  2134)               !! note: convective cloud fraction is used in the radiation, convective water contents are the same as the stratiform scheme.
  2135)               mr_ccliq(i,k) = (state%q(i,k,ixcldliq)/cld(i,k))*concld(i,k)
  2136)               mr_ccice(i,k) = (state%q(i,k,ixcldice)/cld(i,k))*concld(i,k)
  2137)               mr_lsliq(i,k) = (state%q(i,k,ixcldliq)/cld(i,k))*(cld(i,k)-concld(i,k))   ! mr_lsliq, mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)  
  2138)               mr_lsice(i,k) = (state%q(i,k,ixcldice)/cld(i,k))*(cld(i,k)-concld(i,k))   ! mr_lsice - mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  2139)            else
  2140)               mr_ccliq(i,k) = 0._r8
  2141)               mr_ccice(i,k) = 0._r8
  2142)               mr_lsliq(i,k) = 0._r8
  2143)               mr_lsice(i,k) = 0._r8
  2144)            end if
  2145)       end do
  2146)       end do
  2147)  
  2148)       !!! Previously, I had set use_reff=.false.
  2149)       !!! use_reff = .false.  !! if you use this,all sizes use DEFAULT_LIDAR_REFF = 30.0e-6 meters
  2150) 
  2151)       !!! The specification of reff_cosp now follows e-mail discussion with Yuying in January 2011.
  2152)       !!! When there is no reff COSP input, i.e. use_reff=.false., COSP uses reasonable reff defaults for the lidar/radar simulator, respectively. 
  2153)       !!! The lidar simulator uses the default value (30 micron) for clouds, radar simulator uses different defaults.
  2154)       !!! When input radius is 0., the simulated lidar cloud amount will be 0., but the radar simulator will use its internal defaults.
  2155)       !!! We do have size information to give COSP from CAM so I am giving it as much as I can, and setting reff_cosp=0 when no CAM size information is available.
  2156)       !!! Note: setting CVCLIQ=LSCLIQ and CVCICE=LSCICE is not the optimal solution, but if we set them to a specific value the radar simulator will use them
  2157)       !!! and if we set it to 0, the lidar simulator will treat convective clouds as no clouds.  So, we are setting the convective cloud sizes to the
  2158)       !!! large-scale cloud sizes just to have the same reasonablish values entering both the radar and lidar simulator.
  2159) 
  2160)       !!! All of the values that I have assembled in the code are in microns... convert to meters here since that is what COSP wants.
  2161)       use_reff = .true.
  2162)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,1) = rel(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! LSCLIQ
  2163)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,2) = rei(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! LSCICE
  2164)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,3) = 0._r8                        !! LSRAIN (using radar default reff)
  2165)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,4) = 0._r8                        !! LSSNOW (using radar default reff)
  2166)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,5) = rel(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! CVCLIQ (not optimal solution)
  2167)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,6) = rei(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! CVCICE (not optimal solution)
  2168)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,7) = 0._r8                        !! CVRAIN (using radar default reff)
  2169)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,8) = 0._r8                        !! CVSNOW (using radar default reff)
  2170)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,9) = 0._r8                        !! LSGRPL (using radar default reff)
  2171) 
  2172)       !! Need code below for when effective radius is fillvalue, and you multiply it by 1.e-6 to convert units, and value becomes no longer fillvalue.  
  2173)       !! Here, we set it back to zero. ## I think this should this be 0. COSP doesn't know what CAM's fillvalue is... ##2check
  2174)       where (rel(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2175)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,1) = 0._r8
  2176)       end where
  2177)       where (rei(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2178)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,2) = 0._r8
  2179)       end where
  2180)       where (rel(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2181)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,5) = 0._r8
  2182)       end where
  2183)       where (rei(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2184)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,6) = 0._r8
  2185)       end where
  2186) 
  2187)    end if  !!if cam4/cam3
  2188) 
  2189)    if( cam_physpkg_is('cam5') ) then
  2190)       use_precipitation_fluxes = .true.      !!! consistent with cam4 implementation.
  2191) 
  2192)       ! add together deep and shallow convection precipitation fluxes, recall *_flxprc variables are rain+snow
  2193)       rain_cv(1:ncol,1:pverp) = (sh_flxprc(1:ncol,1:pverp)-sh_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp)) + &
  2194)                                 (dp_flxprc(1:ncol,1:pverp)-dp_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp))
  2195)       snow_cv(1:ncol,1:pverp) = sh_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp) + dp_flxsnw(1:ncol,1:pverp)
  2196) 
  2197)       ! interpolate interface precip fluxes to mid points
  2198)       do i=1,ncol
  2199)               ! find weights (pressure weighting?)
  2200)               call lininterp_init(state%zi(i,1:pverp),pverp,state%zm(i,1:pver),pver,extrap_method,interp_wgts)
  2201)               ! interpolate  lininterp1d(arrin, nin, arrout, nout, interp_wgts)
  2202)               ! note: lininterp is an interface, contains lininterp1d -- code figures out to use lininterp1d.
  2203)               call lininterp(rain_cv(i,1:pverp),pverp,rain_cv_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2204)               call lininterp(snow_cv(i,1:pverp),pverp,snow_cv_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2205)               call lininterp(ls_flxprc(i,1:pverp),pverp,rain_ls_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2206)               call lininterp(ls_flxsnw(i,1:pverp),pverp,snow_ls_interp(i,1:pver),pver,interp_wgts)
  2207)               call lininterp_finish(interp_wgts)
  2208)               !! ls_flxprc is for rain+snow, find rain_ls_interp by subtracting off snow_ls_interp
  2209)               rain_ls_interp(i,1:pver)=rain_ls_interp(i,1:pver)-snow_ls_interp(i,1:pver)
  2210)       end do
  2211) 
  2212)       !! CAM5 cloud mixing ratio calculations
  2213)       !! Note: Although CAM5 has non-zero convective cloud mixing ratios that affect the model state, 
  2214)       !! Convective cloud water is NOT part of radiation calculations.
  2215)       do k=1,pver
  2216)       do i=1,ncol
  2217)            if (cld(i,k) .gt. 0._r8) then
  2218)               !! note: convective mixing ratio is the sum of shallow and deep convective clouds in CAM5
  2219)               mr_ccliq(i,k) = sh_cldliq(i,k) + dp_cldliq(i,k)
  2220)               mr_ccice(i,k) = sh_cldliq(i,k) + dp_cldliq(i,k)
  2221)               mr_lsliq(i,k)=state%q(i,k,ixcldliq)   ! mr_lsliq, mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_liquid, state only includes stratiform (kg/kg)  
  2222)               mr_lsice(i,k)=state%q(i,k,ixcldice)   ! mr_lsice - mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_ice, state only includes stratiform (kg/kg)
  2223)            else
  2224)               mr_ccliq(i,k) = 0._r8
  2225)               mr_ccice(i,k) = 0._r8
  2226)               mr_lsliq(i,k) = 0._r8
  2227)               mr_lsice(i,k) = 0._r8
  2228)            end if
  2229)       end do
  2230)       end do
  2231) 
  2232)       !! Previously, I had set use_reff=.false.
  2233)       !! use_reff = .false.  !! if you use this,all sizes use DEFAULT_LIDAR_REFF = 30.0e-6 meters
  2234) 
  2235)       !! The specification of reff_cosp now follows e-mail discussion with Yuying in January 2011. (see above)
  2236)       !! All of the values that I have assembled in the code are in microns... convert to meters here since that is what COSP wants.
  2237)       use_reff = .true.
  2238)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,1) = rel(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8          !! LSCLIQ  (same as effc and effliq in stratiform.F90)
  2239)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,2) = rei(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8          !! LSCICE  (same as effi and effice in stratiform.F90)
  2240)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,3) = ls_reffrain(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! LSRAIN  (calculated in cldwat2m_micro.F90, passed to stratiform.F90)
  2241)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,4) = ls_reffsnow(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! LSSNOW  (calculated in cldwat2m_micro.F90, passed to stratiform.F90)
  2242)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,5) = cv_reffliq(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8   !! CVCLIQ (calculated in stratiform.F90, not actually used in radiation)
  2243)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,6) = cv_reffice(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8   !! CVCICE (calculated in stratiform.F90, not actually used in radiation)
  2244)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,7) = ls_reffrain(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! CVRAIN (same as stratiform per Andrew)
  2245)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,8) = ls_reffsnow(1:ncol,1:pver)*1.e-6_r8  !! CVSNOW (same as stratiform per Andrew)
  2246)       reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,9) = 0._r8                                !! LSGRPL (using radar default reff)
  2247) 
  2248)       !! Need code below for when effective radius is fillvalue, and you multiply it by 1.e-6 to convert units, and value becomes no longer fillvalue.  
  2249)       !! Here, we set it back to zero. 
  2250)       where (rel(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2251)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,1) = 0._r8
  2252)       end where
  2253)       where (rei(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2254)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,2) = 0._r8
  2255)       end where
  2256)       where (ls_reffrain(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2257)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,3) = 0._r8
  2258)       end where
  2259)       where (ls_reffsnow(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2260)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,4) = 0._r8
  2261)       end where
  2262)       where (cv_reffliq(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2263)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,5) = 0._r8
  2264)       end where
  2265)       where (cv_reffice(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2266)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,6) = 0._r8
  2267)       end where
  2268)       where (ls_reffrain(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2269)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,7) = 0._r8
  2270)       end where
  2271)       where (ls_reffsnow(1:ncol,1:pver) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  2272)           reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,8) = 0._r8
  2273)       end where
  2274) 
  2275)    end if  !!if cam5
  2276) 
  2277)    !! Make sure interpolated values are not less than 0 - COSP was complaining and resetting small negative values to zero.
  2278)    !! ----- WARNING: COSP_CHECK_INPUT_2D: minimum value of rain_ls set to:      0.000000000000000 
  2279)    !! So I set negative values to zero here...
  2280)    do k=1,pver
  2281)    do i=1,ncol
  2282)            if (rain_ls_interp(i,k) .lt. 0._r8) then
  2283)                 rain_ls_interp(i,k)=0._r8
  2284)            end if
  2285)            if (snow_ls_interp(i,k) .lt. 0._r8) then
  2286)                 snow_ls_interp(i,k)=0._r8
  2287)            end if
  2288)            if (rain_cv_interp(i,k) .lt. 0._r8) then
  2289)                 rain_cv_interp(i,k)=0._r8
  2290)            end if
  2291)            if (snow_cv_interp(i,k) .lt. 0._r8) then
  2292)                 snow_cv_interp(i,k)=0._r8
  2293)            end if
  2294)    end do
  2295)    end do
  2296) 
  2297) ! 5) assign optical depths and emissivities needed for isccp simulator
  2298) 
  2299)        !! initialize cld_swtau
  2300)        cld_swtau(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8
  2301) 
  2302)        if( cam_physpkg_is('cam4') ) then
  2303)           ! cam4 compute the optical depth (code from radcswmx) -- code from cloudsimulator.F90 (NOW IN CAMRT's radiation.F90
  2304)           do k=1,pver
  2305)           do i=1,ncol
  2306)                   if(cld(i,k) >= cldmin .and. cld(i,k) >= cldeps) then
  2307)                      cld_swtau(i,k) = (abarl + bbarl/rel(i,k)) * cliqwp_in(i,k) + &
  2308)                           (abari + bbari/rei(i,k)) * cicewp_in(i,k)
  2309)                   else
  2310)                      cld_swtau(i,k) = 0._r8
  2311)                   end if
  2312)           end do
  2313)           end do
  2314)        end if
  2315) 
  2316)        if( cam_physpkg_is('cam5') ) then
  2317)             cld_swtau(1:ncol,1:pver) = cld_swtau_in(1:ncol,1:pver)
  2318)        end if
  2319) 
  2320)        ! initialize cosp inputs
  2321)        dtau_s(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8
  2322)        dtau_c(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8
  2323)        dtau_s_snow(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8
  2324)        dem_s(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8 
  2325)        dem_c(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8
  2326)        dem_s_snow(1:ncol,1:pver) = 0._r8 
  2327) 
  2328)        ! assign values
  2329)        ! NOTES:
  2330)        ! 1) CAM4 assumes same radiative properties for stratiform and convective clouds, 
  2331)        ! (see ISCCP_CLOUD_TYPES subroutine call in cloudsimulator.F90)
  2332)        ! I presume CAM5 is doing the same thing based on the ISCCP simulator calls within RRTM's radiation.F90
  2333)        ! 2) COSP wants in-cloud values.  CAM5 values cld_swtau are in-cloud.
  2334)        ! 3) snow_tau_in and snow_emis_in are passed without modification to COSP
  2335) 
  2336)        dtau_s(1:ncol,1:pver) = cld_swtau(1:ncol,1:pver)         ! mean 0.67 micron optical depth of stratiform (in-cloud)
  2337)        dtau_c(1:ncol,1:pver) = cld_swtau(1:ncol,1:pver)         !  mean 0.67 micron optical depth of convective (in-cloud)
  2338)        dem_s(1:ncol,1:pver) = emis(1:ncol,1:pver)               !  10.5 micron longwave emissivity of stratiform (in-cloud)
  2339)        dem_c(1:ncol,1:pver) = emis(1:ncol,1:pver)               !  10.5 micron longwave emissivity of convective (in-cloud)
  2340) ! cam4 physics seg faults if this conditional is not used
  2341)        if( cam_physpkg_is('cam5') ) then
  2342)            dem_s_snow(1:ncol,1:pver) = snow_emis_in(1:ncol,1:pver)      !  10.5 micron grid-box mean optical depth of stratiform snow
  2343)            dtau_s_snow(1:ncol,1:pver) = snow_tau_in(1:ncol,1:pver)      ! 0.67 micron grid-box mean optical depth of stratiform snow
  2344)            !! loop to check values of dem_s_snow
  2345)            !do i=1,ncol
  2346)            !do k=1,pver
  2347)            !    if (dem_s_snow(i,k) > 1._r8) then
  2348)            !       print *, 'PROBLEM with dem_s_snow', dem_s_snow(i,k), i , k
  2349)            !    end if
  2350)            !end do 
  2351)            !end do
  2352)            !!
  2353)        end if
  2354) 
  2355) 
  2356) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2357) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2358) !!!!!!! END TRANSLATE CAM VARIABLES TO COSP INPUT VARIABLES
  2359) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2360) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2361) 
  2362) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2363) ! RUN ALL COSP SIMULATORS ON ALL COLUMNS (COSP SETUP/CALL #1)
  2364) ! This code is invoked when namelist variable "cosp_runall" is set to .true.
  2365) ! I want to keep this functionality because it is useful for testing
  2366) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2367) 
  2368) if (cosp_runall) then
  2369) 
  2370) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2371) !  POPULATE COSP INPUT VARIABLE ("gbx") FROM CAM VARIABLES
  2372) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2373) ! Create and Populate the input structure for COSP - "gbx"
  2374) ! Check cosp_input_nl information for gbx
  2375) ! contruct_* and free_* routines from /home/jenkay/cosp/cosp.v1.1/cosp_types.f90 
  2376) ! allocate and deallocate memory within this module.
  2377) ! gbx %s to set are lon, lat, p, ph, zlev, zlev_half, T, rh, sh, cca, tca, ph, 
  2378)    ! skt, landmask, mr_ozone, u_wind, v_wind, sunlit
  2379)    ! mr_lsliq, mr_lsice, mr_ccliq, mr_ccice, fl_lsrain, fl_lssnow, fl_lsgrpl, 
  2380)    ! fl_ccrain, fl_ccsnow, Reff, dtau_s, dtau_c, dem_s, dem_c, dtau_s_snow, dem_s_snow 
  2381)    ! Make sure that you get cloud information from deep, shallow, and stratiform physics packages.
  2382) 
  2383)    !print *, 'Allocating memory for gridbox type...'
  2384)    call construct_cosp_gridbox(time, &                          ! 1 double precision = real(r8) X
  2385)                                 time_bnds, &                    ! 1 double precision = real(r8)
  2386)                                 radar_freq, &                   ! 2 real(r8) X
  2387)                                 surface_radar, &                ! 3 integer X
  2388)                                 use_mie_tables, &               ! 4 integer X
  2389)                                 use_gas_abs, &                  ! 5 integer X
  2390)                                 do_ray, &                       ! 6 integer X 
  2391)                                 melt_lay, &                     ! 7 integer X 
  2392)                                 k2, &                           ! 8 real(r8) X
  2393)                                 Npoints, &                      ! 9 integer X, same as CAM's ncol
  2394)                                 Nlevels, &                      ! 10 integer X
  2395)                                 ncolumns,&                      ! 11 integer X
  2396)                                 nhydro,&                        ! 12 integer X
  2397)                                 Nprmts_max_hydro,&              ! 13 integer X
  2398)                                 Naero,&                         ! 14 integer X
  2399)                                 Nprmts_max_aero,&               ! 15 integer X
  2400)                                 Npoints_it, &                   ! 16 integer X
  2401)                                 lidar_ice_type,&                ! 17 integer X
  2402)                                 isccp_topheight,&               ! 18 integer X
  2403)                                 isccp_topheight_direction,&     ! 19 integer X
  2404)                                 overlap,&                       ! 20 integer X
  2405)                                 emsfc_lw, &                     ! 21 real X
  2406)                                 use_precipitation_fluxes,&      ! 22 logical X
  2407)                                 use_reff, &                     ! 23 logical X
  2408)                                 Platform, &                     ! 24 integer X
  2409)                                 Satellite, &                    ! 25 integer X
  2410)                                 Instrument, &                   ! 26 integer X
  2411)                                 Nchannels, &                    ! 27 integer X
  2412)                                 ZenAng, &                       ! 28 real(r8) X
  2413)                                 Channels(1:Nchannels),&         ! 29 integer X
  2414)                                 Surfem(1:Nchannels),&           ! 30 real(r8) X
  2415)                                 co2(1,1),&                      ! 31 real(r8) X
  2416)                                 ch4(1,1),&                      ! 32 real(r8) X
  2417)                                 n2o(1,1),&                      ! 33 real(r8) X
  2418)                                 co,&                            ! 34 real(r8) X
  2419)                                 gbx)                            ! OUT
  2420)     
  2421)    !print *, 'Populating input structure for COSP...'
  2422)    ! Note: GBX expects vertical ordering to be from SURFACE(1) to the TOP(nlev), while
  2423)    ! by default CAM uses TOP(1) to SURFACE(nlev).
  2424)    ! also gbx is by definition of size ncol, but many variables defined as pcol.  be explicit here, gbx = 1:ncol
  2425) 
  2426)    gbx%longitude = lon_cosp(1:ncol)                             ! lon (degrees_east)
  2427)    gbx%latitude = lat_cosp(1:ncol)                              ! lat (degrees_north)
  2428) ! look at cosp_types.F90 in v1.3 for information on how these should be defined.
  2429)    gbx%p = state%pmid(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                         ! Pressure at full model levels [Pa] (at model levels per yuying)
  2430)    gbx%ph = pbot(1:ncol,1:pver)                                 ! Pressure at half model levels [Pa] (Bottom of model layer,flipped above)
  2431)    gbx%zlev = zmid(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                            ! Height of model midpoint levels asl [m] (at model levels)
  2432)    gbx%zlev_half = zbot(1:ncol,1:pver)                          ! Height at half model levels asl [m] (Bottom of model layer, flipped above)
  2433)    gbx%T = state%t(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                            ! air_temperature (K)
  2434)    gbx%q = rh(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                                 ! relative humidity wrt water 
  2435)                                                                 ! note: it is confusing that it is called "q" within cosp,
  2436)                                                                 ! but it is rh according to Yuying
  2437)    gbx%sh = q(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                                 ! specific humidity (kg/kg), range [0,0.019ish]
  2438)    gbx%cca = concld(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                           ! convective_cloud_amount (0-1)
  2439)    gbx%tca = cld(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                              ! total_cloud_amount (0-1)
  2440)    gbx%psfc = state%ps(1:ncol)                                  ! surface pressure (Pa)
  2441)    gbx%skt  = cam_in%ts(1:ncol)                                 ! skin temperature (K)
  2442)    gbx%land = landmask(1:ncol)                                  ! landmask (0 or 1)
  2443)    gbx%mr_ozone  = o3(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                         ! ozone mass mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  2444)    gbx%u_wind  = state%u(1:ncol,pver)                           ! surface u_wind (m/s)
  2445)    gbx%v_wind  = state%v(1:ncol,pver)                           ! surface v_wind (m/s)
  2446)    gbx%sunlit  = 1                                              !  ??? what does this mean??
  2447)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_LSCLIQ) = mr_lsliq(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)      ! mr_lsliq, mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)  
  2448)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_LSCICE) = mr_lsice(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)      ! mr_lsice - mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  2449)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_CVCLIQ) = mr_ccliq(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)      ! mr_ccliq - mixing_ratio_convective_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)
  2450)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_CVCICE) = mr_ccice(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)      ! mr_ccice - mixing_ratio_convective_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  2451)    gbx%rain_ls = rain_ls_interp(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)               ! midpoint gbm ls rain flux  (kg m^-2 s^-1)
  2452)    gbx%snow_ls = snow_ls_interp(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)               ! midpoint gbm ls snow flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)      
  2453)    gbx%grpl_ls = grpl_ls_interp(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)               ! midpoint gbm ls graupel flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
  2454)    gbx%rain_cv = rain_cv_interp(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)               ! midpoint gbm conv rain flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
  2455)    gbx%snow_cv = snow_cv_interp(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)               ! midpoint gbm conv snow flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
  2456)    gbx%Reff = reff_cosp(1:ncol,pver:1:-1,:)                     ! Effective radius [m]
  2457)    gbx%dtau_s   = dtau_s(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                      ! mean 0.67 micron optical depth of stratiform
  2458)                                                                 !  clouds in each model level
  2459)                                                                 !  NOTE:  this the cloud optical depth of only the
  2460)                                                                 !  cloudy part of the grid box, it is not weighted
  2461)                                                                 !  with the 0 cloud optical depth of the clear
  2462)                                                                 !  part of the grid box
  2463)    gbx%dtau_c   = dtau_c(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                      !  mean 0.67 micron optical depth of convective
  2464)    gbx%dtau_s_snow   = dtau_s_snow(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)            !  grid-box mean 0.67 micron optical depth of stratiform snow
  2465)    gbx%dem_s    = dem_s(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                       !  10.5 micron longwave emissivity of stratiform cloud
  2466)    gbx%dem_c    = dem_c(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                       !  10.5 micron longwave emissivity of convective cloud
  2467)    gbx%dem_s_snow = dem_s_snow(1:ncol,pver:1:-1)                !  10.5 micron grid-box mean optical depth of stratiform snow
  2468) 
  2469) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2470) ! STARTUP RELATED TO COSP OUTPUT (see cosp.F90)
  2471) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2472) ! Note: COSP output variables are sgx (sub-grid outputs), sgradar (radar outputs), sglidar (lidar outputs), 
  2473) ! isccp (isccp outputs), misr (misr simulator outputs), vgrid (vertical grid info), stradar 
  2474) ! (summary statistics radar simulator), stlidar (summary statistics lidar simulator)
  2475) 
  2476) ! Define new vertical grid
  2477)    !print *, 'Defining new vertical grid...'
  2478)    call construct_cosp_vgrid(gbx,nlr,use_vgrid,csat_vgrid,vgrid)
  2479)         
  2480) ! Allocate memory for output
  2481)    !print *, 'Allocating memory for other types...'
  2482)    call construct_cosp_subgrid(Npoints, ncolumns, Nlevels, sgx)
  2483)    call construct_cosp_sgradar(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,nhydro,sgradar)
  2484)    call construct_cosp_radarstats(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,vgrid%Nlvgrid,nhydro,stradar)
  2485)    call construct_cosp_sglidar(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,nhydro,PARASOL_NREFL,sglidar)
  2486)    call construct_cosp_lidarstats(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,vgrid%Nlvgrid,nhydro,PARASOL_NREFL,stlidar)
  2487)    call construct_cosp_isccp(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,isccp)
  2488)    call construct_cosp_misr(cfg,Npoints,misr)
  2489)    !! new for cosp v1.3
  2490)    call construct_cosp_modis(cfg,Npoints,modis)
  2491) 
  2492) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2493) !  RUN COSP on all columns
  2494) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2495) 
  2496)    if (cosp_histfile_aux) then
  2497)       call outfld('PS_COSP',gbx%psfc,ncol,lchnk)
  2498)       call outfld('TS_COSP',gbx%skt,ncol,lchnk)
  2499)       call outfld ('P_COSP',gbx%p(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2500)       call outfld ('PH_COSP',gbx%ph(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2501)       call outfld ('ZLEV_COSP',gbx%zlev(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2502)       call outfld ('ZLEV_HALF_COSP',gbx%zlev_half(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2503)       call outfld('T_COSP',gbx%T(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2504)       call outfld('RH_COSP',gbx%q(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2505)       call outfld('Q_COSP',gbx%sh(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2506)       call outfld('CONCLD_COSP',gbx%cca(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2507)       call outfld('CLD_COSP',gbx%tca(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2508)       call outfld('O3_COSP',gbx%mr_ozone(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2509)       call outfld('U_COSP',gbx%u_wind,ncol,lchnk)
  2510)       call outfld('V_COSP',gbx%v_wind,ncol,lchnk)
  2511)       call outfld('LSCLIQ_COSP',gbx%mr_hydro(:,pver:1:-1,I_LSCLIQ),ncol,lchnk)
  2512)       call outfld('LSCICE_COSP',gbx%mr_hydro(:,pver:1:-1,I_LSCICE),ncol,lchnk)
  2513)       call outfld('CVCLIQ_COSP',gbx%mr_hydro(:,pver:1:-1,I_CVCLIQ),ncol,lchnk)
  2514)       call outfld('CVCICE_COSP',gbx%mr_hydro(:,pver:1:-1,I_CVCICE),ncol,lchnk)
  2515)       call outfld('RAIN_LS_COSP',gbx%rain_ls(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2516)       call outfld('SNOW_LS_COSP',gbx%snow_ls(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2517)       call outfld('GRPL_LS_COSP',gbx%grpl_ls(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2518)       call outfld('RAIN_CV_COSP',gbx%rain_cv(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2519)       call outfld('SNOW_CV_COSP',gbx%snow_cv(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2520)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_1',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,1),ncol,lchnk)
  2521)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_2',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,2),ncol,lchnk)
  2522)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_3',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,3),ncol,lchnk)
  2523)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_4',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,4),ncol,lchnk)
  2524)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_5',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,5),ncol,lchnk)
  2525)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_6',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,6),ncol,lchnk)
  2526)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_7',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,7),ncol,lchnk)
  2527)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_8',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,8),ncol,lchnk)
  2528)       call outfld('REFF_COSP_9',gbx%Reff(:,pver:1:-1,9),ncol,lchnk)
  2529)       call outfld('DTAU_S_COSP',gbx%dtau_s(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2530)       call outfld('DTAU_C_COSP',gbx%dtau_c(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2531)       call outfld('DEM_S_COSP',gbx%dem_s(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2532)       call outfld('DEM_C_COSP',gbx%dem_c(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2533)       call outfld('DTAU_S_COSP_SNOW',gbx%dtau_s_snow(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2534)       call outfld('DEM_S_COSP_SNOW',gbx%dem_s_snow(1:ncol,pver:1:-1),ncol,lchnk)
  2535)    end if
  2536) 
  2537)    !print *, 'Calling the COSP simulator and running on all columns...'
  2538)    call cosp(overlap,ncolumns,cfg,vgrid,gbx,sgx,sgradar,sglidar,isccp,misr,modis,stradar,stlidar)
  2539) 
  2540) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2541) !  TRANSLATE COSP OUTPUT INTO INDIVIDUAL VARIABLES FOR OUTPUT (see nc_write_cosp_1d in cosp_io.f90)
  2542) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2543) 
  2544)    ! Populate CAM vars with COSP output (the reasoning for this is based on cosp_io.f90)
  2545)    ! (1d variables)
  2546)    cldlow_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,1)           ! CAM version of cllcalipso (time,profile)      
  2547)    cldmed_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,2)           ! CAM version of clmcalipso (time,profile)
  2548)    cldhgh_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,3)           ! CAM version of clhcalipso (time,profile)
  2549)    cldtot_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,4)           ! CAM version of cltcalipso (time,profile)
  2550)    cldtot_calcs(1:ncol) = stradar%radar_lidar_tcc       ! CAM version of cltlidarradar (time,profile)
  2551)    cldtot_cs(1:ncol) = stradar%radar_tcc                ! CAM version of cltradar (time,profile)
  2552)    cldtot_cs2(1:ncol) = stradar%radar_tcc_2             ! CAM version of cltradar2 (time,profile)
  2553)    cldtot_isccp(1:ncol) = isccp%totalcldarea            ! CAM version of tclisccp (time,profile)
  2554)    meanptop_isccp(1:ncol) = isccp%meanptop              ! CAM version of ctpisccp (time,profile)
  2555)    meantau_isccp(1:ncol) = isccp%meantaucld             ! CAM version of meantbisccp (time,profile)
  2556)    meancldalb_isccp(1:ncol) = isccp%meanalbedocld       ! CAM version of albisccp (time,profile)
  2557)    meantb_isccp(1:ncol) = isccp%meantb                  ! CAM version of meantbisccp (time,profile)
  2558)    meantbclr_isccp(1:ncol) = isccp%meantbclr            ! CAM version of meantbclrisccp (time,profile)
  2559)    ! (2d variables)
  2560)    cld_cal(1:ncol,1:nht_cosp) = stlidar%lidarcld                        ! CAM version of clcalipso (time,height,profile)
  2561)    cld_cal_notcs(1:ncol,1:nht_cosp) = stradar%lidar_only_freq_cloud     ! CAM version of clcalipso2 (time,height,profile)
  2562)    mol532_cal(1:ncol,1:nhtml_cosp) = sglidar%beta_mol                   ! CAM version of beta_mol532 (time,height_mlev,profile)
  2563)    tau_isccp(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp) = isccp%boxtau                        ! CAM version of boxtauisccp (time,column,profile)
  2564)    cldptop_isccp(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp) = isccp%boxptop                   ! CAM version of boxptopisccp (time,column,profile)
  2565)    refl_parasol(1:ncol,1:nsza_cosp) = stlidar%parasolrefl               ! CAM version of parasolrefl (time,sza,profile)
  2566)    ! (3d variables)
  2567)    dbze94(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp) = sgradar%Ze_tot            ! dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  2568)    atb532(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp) = sglidar%beta_tot          ! atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  2569)    frac_out(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp) = sgx%frac_out            ! frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  2570)    cfad_dbze94(1:ncol,1:ndbze_cosp,1:nht_cosp) = stradar%cfad_ze        ! cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile)
  2571)    cfad_lidarsr532(1:ncol,1:nsr_cosp,1:nht_cosp)= stlidar%cfad_sr       ! cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  2572)    clisccp2(1:ncol,1:ntau_cosp,1:nprs_cosp) = isccp%fq_isccp            ! clisccp2 (time,tau,plev,profile)
  2573)    clMISR(1:ncol,1:ntau_cosp,1:nhtmisr_cosp) = misr%fq_MISR             ! clMISR (time,tau,CTH_height_bin,profile)
  2574)    !! modis variables
  2575)    cltmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Fraction_Total_Mean
  2576)    clwmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Fraction_Water_Mean
  2577)    climodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Fraction_Ice_Mean
  2578)    clhmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Fraction_High_Mean
  2579)    clmmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Fraction_Mid_Mean
  2580)    cllmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Fraction_Low_Mean
  2581)    tautmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Optical_Thickness_Total_Mean
  2582)    tauwmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Optical_Thickness_Water_Mean
  2583)    tauimodis(1:ncol)=modis%Optical_Thickness_Ice_Mean
  2584)    tautlogmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Optical_Thickness_Total_LogMean
  2585)    tauwlogmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Optical_Thickness_Water_LogMean
  2586)    tauilogmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Optical_Thickness_Ice_LogMean
  2587)    reffclwmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Particle_Size_Water_Mean
  2588)    reffclimodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Particle_Size_Ice_Mean
  2589)    pctmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Cloud_Top_Pressure_Total_Mean
  2590)    lwpmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Liquid_Water_Path_Mean
  2591)    iwpmodis(1:ncol)=modis%Ice_Water_Path_Mean
  2592)    clmodis(1:ncol,1:ntau_cosp_modis,1:nprs_cosp)=modis%Optical_Thickness_vs_Cloud_Top_Pressure
  2593) 
  2594)    !print *, 'Done mapping COSP output to local variables ...'
  2595) 
  2596)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  2597)    ! see above for mixed dimension definitions
  2598)    ! i am using the convention of starting vertical coordinates at the surface, up to down, COSP convention, not CAM.
  2599) 
  2600)    do i=1,ncol
  2601) 
  2602)         ! CAM cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile) 
  2603)         do ih=1,nht_cosp
  2604)         do id=1,ndbze_cosp
  2605)            ihd=(ih-1)*ndbze_cosp+id                     
  2606)            cfad_dbze94_cs(i,ihd) = cfad_dbze94(i,id,ih)         ! cfad_dbze94_cs(pcols,nht_cosp*ndbze_cosp)
  2607)         end do
  2608)         end do
  2609)         ! CAM cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  2610)         do ih=1,nht_cosp
  2611)         do is=1,nsr_cosp
  2612)            ihs=(ih-1)*nsr_cosp+is                       
  2613)            cfad_sr532_cal(i,ihs) = cfad_lidarsr532(i,is,ih)  ! cfad_sr532_cal(pcols,nht_cosp*nsr_cosp)
  2614)         end do
  2615)         end do
  2616)         ! CAM dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  2617)         do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  2618)         do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  2619)            ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                 
  2620)            dbze_cs(i,ihsc) = dbze94(i,isc,ihml)                 ! dbze_cs(pcols,pver*nscol_cosp) 
  2621)         end do
  2622)         end do
  2623)         ! CAM clMISR (time,tau,CTH_height_bin,profile)
  2624)         do ihm=1,nhtmisr_cosp
  2625)         do it=1,ntau_cosp
  2626)            ihmt=(ihm-1)*ntau_cosp+it                    
  2627)            cld_misr(i,ihmt) = clMISR(i,it,ihm)                  ! cld_misr(pcols,nhtmisr_cosp*ntau_cosp)
  2628)         end do
  2629)         end do
  2630)         ! CAM atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)  FIX
  2631)         do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  2632)         do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  2633)            ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                 
  2634)            atb532_cal(i,ihsc) = atb532(i,isc,ihml)              ! atb532_cal(pcols,nht_cosp*nscol_cosp)
  2635)         end do
  2636)         end do
  2637)         ! CAM frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)  FIX
  2638)         do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  2639)         do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  2640)            ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                 
  2641)            scops_out(i,ihsc) = frac_out(i,isc,ihml)             ! scops_out(pcols,nht_cosp*nscol_cosp)
  2642)         end do
  2643)         end do
  2644)         ! CAM clmodis
  2645)         do ip=1,nprs_cosp
  2646)         do it=1,ntau_cosp_modis
  2647)            ipt=(ip-1)*ntau_cosp_modis+it
  2648)            clmodis_cam(i,ipt) = clmodis(i,it,ip)
  2649)         end do
  2650)         end do
  2651)    end do
  2652) 
  2653) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2654) ! DEALLOCATE MEMORY for running with all columns
  2655) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2656)    call free_cosp_gridbox(gbx)
  2657)    call free_cosp_vgrid(vgrid)
  2658)    call free_cosp_subgrid(sgx)
  2659)    call free_cosp_sgradar(sgradar)
  2660)    call free_cosp_radarstats(stradar)
  2661)    call free_cosp_sglidar(sglidar)
  2662)    call free_cosp_lidarstats(stlidar)
  2663)    call free_cosp_isccp(isccp)
  2664)    call free_cosp_misr(misr) 
  2665)    call free_cosp_modis(modis)
  2666) 
  2667) end if !! if cosp_runall
  2668) 
  2669) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2670) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2671) !  RUN COSP ONLY ON SUNLIT COLUMNS FOR ISCCP and/or MISR and/or MODIS SIMULATORS (COSP SETUP/CALL #2)
  2672) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2673) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2674) 
  2675) if ((.not.cosp_runall) .and. (lisccp_sim.or.lmisr_sim.or.lmodis_sim)) then  !! RUNNING ON SUNLIT
  2676) 
  2677)    cfg%Lalbisccp=lalbisccp
  2678)    cfg%Latb532=latb532
  2679)    cfg%Lboxptopisccp=lboxptopisccp
  2680)    cfg%Lboxtauisccp=lboxtauisccp
  2681)    cfg%Lcfaddbze94=lcfad_dbze94
  2682)    cfg%LcfadLidarsr532=lcfad_lidarsr532
  2683)    cfg%Lclcalipso=lclcalipso
  2684)    cfg%Lclhcalipso=lclhcalipso
  2685)    cfg%Lclisccp=lclisccp2
  2686)    cfg%Lcllcalipso=lcllcalipso
  2687)    cfg%Lclmcalipso=lclmcalipso
  2688)    cfg%Lcltcalipso=lcltcalipso
  2689)    cfg%Lpctisccp=lctpisccp
  2690)    cfg%Ldbze94=ldbze94
  2691)    cfg%Lcltradar=lcltradar
  2692)    cfg%Lcltradar2=lcltradar2
  2693)    cfg%Ltauisccp=ltauisccp
  2694)    cfg%Lcltisccp=ltclisccp
  2695)    cfg%Llongitude=llongitude
  2696)    cfg%Llatitude=llatitude
  2697)    cfg%LparasolRefl=lparasol_refl
  2698)    cfg%LclMISR=lclMISR
  2699)    cfg%Lmeantbisccp=lmeantbisccp
  2700)    cfg%Lmeantbclrisccp=lmeantbclrisccp
  2701)    cfg%Lclcalipso2=lclcalipso2
  2702)    cfg%Lcltlidarradar=lcltlidarradar
  2703)    cfg%Lfracout=lfrac_out
  2704)    cfg%LlidarBetaMol532=lbeta_mol532
  2705) 
  2706) ! Only run the isccp and misr simulators
  2707) if (lisccp_sim.or.lmodis_sim) then
  2708)    cfg%Lisccp_sim= .true.
  2709)    cfg%Lalbisccp= .true.
  2710)    cfg%Latb532= .true.
  2711)    cfg%Lboxptopisccp= .true.
  2712)    cfg%Lboxtauisccp= .true.
  2713)    cfg%Lpctisccp= .true.
  2714)    cfg%Ltauisccp= .true.
  2715)    cfg%Lcltisccp= .true.
  2716)    cfg%Lmeantbisccp= .true.
  2717)    cfg%Lmeantbclrisccp= .true.
  2718) end if
  2719) if (lmisr_sim) then
  2720)    cfg%Lmisr_sim= .true.
  2721)    cfg%LclMISR= .true.
  2722) end if
  2723) if (lmodis_sim) then
  2724)    cfg%Lmodis_sim= .true.
  2725)    cfg%Lcltmodis= .true.
  2726)    cfg%Lclwmodis= .true.
  2727)    cfg%Lclimodis= .true.
  2728)    cfg%Lclhmodis= .true.
  2729)    cfg%Lclmmodis= .true.
  2730)    cfg%Lcllmodis= .true.
  2731)    cfg%Ltautmodis= .true.
  2732)    cfg%Ltauwmodis= .true.
  2733)    cfg%Ltauimodis= .true.
  2734)    cfg%Ltautlogmodis= .true.
  2735)    cfg%Ltauwlogmodis= .true.
  2736)    cfg%Ltauilogmodis= .true.
  2737)    cfg%Lreffclwmodis= .true.
  2738)    cfg%Lreffclimodis= .true.
  2739)    cfg%Lpctmodis= .true.
  2740)    cfg%Llwpmodis= .true.
  2741)    cfg%Liwpmodis= .true.
  2742)    cfg%Lclmodis= .true.
  2743) end if
  2744) 
  2745) ! Don't run the radar/lidar simulators by setting COSP input structure cfg
  2746) cfg%Lradar_sim= .false.
  2747) cfg%Llidar_sim= .false.
  2748) 
  2749) ! Also set radar/lidar/modis simulator outputs to false in COSP input structure cfg
  2750) cfg%Latb532= .false.
  2751) cfg%Lcfaddbze94= .false.
  2752) cfg%LcfadLidarsr532= .false.
  2753) cfg%Lclcalipso= .false.
  2754) cfg%Lclhcalipso= .false.
  2755) cfg%Lcllcalipso= .false.
  2756) cfg%Lclmcalipso= .false.
  2757) cfg%Lcltcalipso= .false.
  2758) cfg%Ldbze94= .false.
  2759) cfg%Lcltradar= .false.
  2760) cfg%Lcltradar2= .false.
  2761) cfg%LparasolRefl= .false.
  2762) cfg%Lclcalipso2= .false.
  2763) cfg%Lcltlidarradar= .false.
  2764) cfg%LlidarBetaMol532= .false.
  2765) 
  2766) ! Don't run cosp_stats.f90, only for radar and lidar
  2767) cfg%Lstats = .false.
  2768) 
  2769) ! Subsetting using the TOD restriction
  2770)     ! Gather night/day column indices. (code from radsw.F90)
  2771)     Nday = 0
  2772)     Nno = 0
  2773)     do i = 1, ncol
  2774) ! adding restrictions here testing, figure out if daylit and run_cosp criterion are met
  2775)        if ((coszrs(i) > 0.0_r8) .and. (run_cosp(i,lchnk))) then
  2776)           Nday = Nday + 1
  2777)           IdxDay(Nday) = i
  2778)        else
  2779)           Nno = Nno + 1
  2780)           IdxNo(Nno) = i
  2781)        end if
  2782)     end do
  2783) 
  2784) ! Reset the number of points for input into COSP
  2785) Npoints = Nday
  2786) 
  2787) if (Nday .gt. 0) then  !! only run COSP if there are daylight points
  2788) 
  2789) !!! rearrange input arrays - compress arrays so that COSP only runs on sunlit columns
  2790) !e.g., a la
  2791) !   call CmpDayNite(E_pmid, pmid,       Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2792) ! (function from ..atm/cam/src/physics/cam/cmparray_mod.F90, see also radsw.F90)
  2793) !! CmpDayNite_2d_R_Copy(InArray, OutArray...
  2794) 
  2795) call CmpDayNite(lon_cosp,lon_cosp_day,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2796) call CmpDayNite(lat_cosp,lat_cosp_day,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2797) call CmpDayNite(ptop, ptop_day,         Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2798) call CmpDayNite(state%pmid, pmid_day,   Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2799) call CmpDayNite(ztop,ztop_day,          Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2800) call CmpDayNite(zmid, zmid_day, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2801) call CmpDayNite(state%t,t_day,          Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2802) call CmpDayNite(rh, rh_day,             Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2803) call CmpDayNite(q, q_day,               Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2804) call CmpDayNite(concld, concld_day,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2805) call CmpDayNite(cld, cld_day,           Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2806) call CmpDayNite(state%ps ,ps_day,       Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2807) call CmpDayNite(cam_in%ts ,ts_day,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2808) call CmpDayNite(landmask,landmask_day,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2809) call CmpDayNite(o3, o3_day,             Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2810) call CmpDayNite(state%u(1:ncol,pver),us_day,            Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, ncol)
  2811) call CmpDayNite(state%v(1:ncol,pver),vs_day,            Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, ncol)
  2812) call CmpDayNite(mr_lsliq,mr_lsliq_day,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2813) call CmpDayNite(mr_lsice,mr_lsice_day,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2814) call CmpDayNite(mr_ccliq, mr_ccliq_day, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2815) call CmpDayNite(mr_ccice, mr_ccice_day, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2816) call CmpDayNite(rain_ls_interp, rain_ls_interp_day,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2817) call CmpDayNite(snow_ls_interp, snow_ls_interp_day,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2818) call CmpDayNite(grpl_ls_interp, grpl_ls_interp_day,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2819) call CmpDayNite(rain_cv_interp,rain_cv_interp_day,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)                    
  2820) call CmpDayNite(snow_cv_interp,snow_cv_interp_day,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2821) call CmpDayNite(dtau_s,dtau_s_day,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2822) call CmpDayNite(dtau_c,dtau_c_day,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2823) call CmpDayNite(dtau_s_snow,dtau_s_snow_day,    Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2824) call CmpDayNite(dem_s,dem_s_day,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2825) call CmpDayNite(dem_c,dem_c_day,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2826) call CmpDayNite(dem_s_snow,dem_s_snow_day,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2827) 
  2828) !! need to loop over nhydro for reff_cosp_day
  2829) do i=1,nhydro
  2830)    call CmpDayNite(reff_cosp(:,:,i),tmp1,               Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  2831)    reff_cosp_day(:,:,i)=tmp1
  2832)    tmp1(1:pcols,1:pver)=R_UNDEF
  2833) end do
  2834) 
  2835) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2836) !  POPULATE COSP INPUT VARIABLE ("gbx") FROM CAM VARIABLES for sunlit columns
  2837) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2838)    !print *, 'Allocating memory for gridbox type for isccp sub-columns only...'
  2839)    call construct_cosp_gridbox(time, &                          ! 1 double precision = real(r8) X
  2840)                                 time_bnds, &                    ! 1 double precision = real(r8)
  2841)                                 radar_freq, &                   ! 2 real(r8) X
  2842)                                 surface_radar, &                ! 3 integer X
  2843)                                 use_mie_tables, &               ! 4 integer X
  2844)                                 use_gas_abs, &                  ! 5 integer X
  2845)                                 do_ray, &                       ! 6 integer X 
  2846)                                 melt_lay, &                     ! 7 integer X 
  2847)                                 k2, &                           ! 8 real(r8) X
  2848)                                 Npoints, &                      ! 9 integer X
  2849)                                 Nlevels, &                      ! 10 integer X
  2850)                                 ncolumns,&                      ! 11 integer X
  2851)                                 nhydro,&                        ! 12 integer X
  2852)                                 Nprmts_max_hydro,&              ! 13 integer X
  2853)                                 Naero,&                         ! 14 integer X
  2854)                                 Nprmts_max_aero,&               ! 15 integer X
  2855)                                 Npoints_it, &                   ! 16 integer X
  2856)                                 lidar_ice_type,&                ! 17 integer X
  2857)                                 isccp_topheight,&               ! 18 integer X
  2858)                                 isccp_topheight_direction,&     ! 19 integer X
  2859)                                 overlap,&                       ! 20 integer X
  2860)                                 emsfc_lw, &                     ! 21 real X
  2861)                                 use_precipitation_fluxes,&      ! 22 logical X
  2862)                                 use_reff, &                     ! 23 logical X
  2863)                                 Platform, &                     ! 24 integer X
  2864)                                 Satellite, &                    ! 25 integer X
  2865)                                 Instrument, &                   ! 26 integer X
  2866)                                 Nchannels, &                    ! 27 integer X
  2867)                                 ZenAng, &                       ! 28 real(r8) X
  2868)                                 Channels(1:Nchannels),&         ! 29 integer X
  2869)                                 Surfem(1:Nchannels),&           ! 30 real(r8) X
  2870)                                 co2(1,1),&                      ! 31 real(r8) X
  2871)                                 ch4(1,1),&                      ! 32 real(r8) X
  2872)                                 n2o(1,1),&                      ! 33 real(r8) X
  2873)                                 co,&                            ! 34 real(r8) X
  2874)                                 gbx)                            ! OUT
  2875)     
  2876)    !print *, 'Populating input structure for COSP running on day columns only...'
  2877)    !! be very explicit about gbx structure sizes.
  2878)    !! flip vertical dimension from COSP convention to CAM convention
  2879)    !! variables initialzed as having 1:pcols dimension, but gbx only wants 1:Nday.
  2880) 
  2881)    gbx%longitude = lon_cosp_day(1:Nday)                         ! lon (degrees_east)
  2882)    gbx%latitude = lat_cosp_day(1:Nday)                          ! lat (degrees_north)
  2883)    gbx%p = ptop_day(1:Nday,1:pver)                              ! p_in_full_levels (Pa),upper interface (flipping done above)
  2884)    gbx%ph = pmid_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                          ! p_in_half_levels (Pa)
  2885)    gbx%zlev = ztop_day(1:Nday,1:pver)                           ! height_in_full_levels (m),upper interface,asl (flipping done above)
  2886)    gbx%zlev_half = zmid_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                   ! height_in_half_levels (m),asl
  2887)    gbx%T = t_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                              ! air_temperature (K)
  2888)    gbx%q = rh_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                             ! relative humidity wrt water 
  2889)                                                                 ! note: it is confusing that it is called "q" within cosp,
