  2890)                                                                 ! but it is rh according to Yuying
  2891)    gbx%sh = q_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                             ! specific humidity (kg/kg), range [0,0.019ish]
  2892)    gbx%cca = concld_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                       ! convective_cloud_amount (0-1)
  2893)    gbx%tca = cld_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                          ! total_cloud_amount (0-1)
  2894)    gbx%psfc = ps_day(1:Nday)                                    ! surface pressure (Pa)
  2895)    gbx%skt  = ts_day(1:Nday)                                    ! skin temperature (K)
  2896)    gbx%land = landmask_day(1:Nday)                              ! landmask (0 or 1)
  2897)    gbx%mr_ozone  = o3_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)                     ! ozone mass mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  2898)    gbx%u_wind  = us_day(1:Nday)                                 ! surface u_wind (m/s)
  2899)    gbx%v_wind  = vs_day(1:Nday)                                 ! surface v_wind (m/s)
  2900)    gbx%sunlit  = 1
  2901)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_LSCLIQ) = mr_lsliq_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)  ! mr_lsliq, mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)
  2902)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_LSCICE) = mr_lsice_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)  ! mr_lsice - mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  2903)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_CVCLIQ) = mr_ccliq_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)  ! mr_ccliq - mixing_ratio_convective_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)
  2904)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_CVCICE) = mr_ccice_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)  ! mr_ccice - mixing_ratio_convective_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  2905)    gbx%rain_ls = rain_ls_interp_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)           ! midpoint gbm
  2906)    gbx%snow_ls = snow_ls_interp_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)           ! midpoint gbm                  
  2907)    gbx%grpl_ls = grpl_ls_interp_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)           ! midpoint gbm
  2908)    gbx%rain_cv = rain_cv_interp_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)           ! midpoint gbm
  2909)    gbx%snow_cv = snow_cv_interp_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)           ! midpoint gbm
  2910)    gbx%Reff = reff_cosp_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1,:)
  2911)    gbx%dtau_s   = dtau_s_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)
  2912)    gbx%dtau_c   = dtau_c_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)
  2913)    gbx%dtau_s_snow   = dtau_s_snow_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)
  2914)    gbx%dem_s    = dem_s_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)
  2915)    gbx%dem_c    = dem_c_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)
  2916)    gbx%dem_s_snow  = dem_s_snow_day(1:Nday,pver:1:-1)
  2917) 
  2918) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2919) ! STARTUP RELATED TO COSP OUTPUT (see cosp.F90) for sunlit columns
  2920) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2921) ! Note: COSP output variables are sgx (sub-grid outputs), sgradar (radar outputs), sglidar (lidar outputs), 
  2922) ! isccp (isccp outputs), misr (misr simulator outputs), vgrid (vertical grid info), stradar 
  2923) ! (summary statistics radar simulator), stlidar (summary statistics lidar simulator)
  2924) 
  2925) ! Define new vertical grid
  2926)    !print *, 'Defining new vertical grid...'
  2927)    call construct_cosp_vgrid(gbx,nlr,use_vgrid,csat_vgrid,vgrid)
  2928)         
  2929) ! Allocate memory for output
  2930)    !print *, 'Allocating memory for other types...'
  2931)    call construct_cosp_subgrid(Npoints, ncolumns, Nlevels, sgx)
  2932)    call construct_cosp_sgradar(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,nhydro,sgradar)
  2933)    call construct_cosp_radarstats(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,vgrid%Nlvgrid,nhydro,stradar)
  2934)    call construct_cosp_sglidar(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,nhydro,PARASOL_NREFL,sglidar)
  2935)    call construct_cosp_lidarstats(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,vgrid%Nlvgrid,nhydro,PARASOL_NREFL,stlidar)
  2936)    call construct_cosp_isccp(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,isccp)
  2937)    call construct_cosp_misr(cfg,Npoints,misr)
  2938)    !! new for cosp v1.3
  2939)    call construct_cosp_modis(cfg,Npoints,modis)
  2940) 
  2941) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2942) !  RUN COSP only on sunlit columns
  2943) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2944) 
  2945)    !print *, 'Calling the COSP simulator and running on sunlit columns...'
  2946)    call cosp(overlap,ncolumns,cfg,vgrid,gbx,sgx,sgradar,sglidar,isccp,misr,modis,stradar,stlidar)
  2947) 
  2948) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2949) !  TRANSLATE COSP OUTPUT INTO INDIVIDUAL VARIABLES FOR OUTPUT (see nc_write_cosp_1d in cosp_io.f90)
  2950) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  2951) 
  2952)    ! Populate CAM vars with COSP output (the reasoning for this is based on cosp_io.f90)
  2953)    !! steps 1) set as fill value, 2) fill in the columns calculated by COSP, 3) expand array
  2954)    !! only do this for the isccp-related and misr output
  2955)    !!! populate variables with fill values where COSP didn't run.
  2956)    ! Note: To expand to output CAM arrays, use ExpDayNite (function from ..atm/cam/src/physics/cam/cmparray_mod.F90, see also radsw.F90)
  2957)    ! e.g.,    call ExpDayNite(solin,    Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2958)    !   call ExpDayNite(pmxrgn,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pverp)
  2959) 
  2960) if (lisccp_sim) then
  2961)    ! (1d variables)
  2962)    cldtot_isccp(1:Nday) = isccp%totalcldarea
  2963)    call ExpDayNite(cldtot_isccp,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2964) 
  2965)    meanptop_isccp(1:Nday) = isccp%meanptop
  2966)    call ExpDayNite(meanptop_isccp,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2967) 
  2968)    meantau_isccp(1:Nday) = isccp%meantaucld
  2969)    call ExpDayNite(meantau_isccp,       Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2970) 
  2971)    meancldalb_isccp(1:Nday) = isccp%meanalbedocld
  2972)    call ExpDayNite(meancldalb_isccp,    Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2973) 
  2974)    meantb_isccp(1:Nday) = isccp%meantb
  2975)    call ExpDayNite(meantb_isccp,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2976) 
  2977)    meantbclr_isccp(1:Nday) = isccp%meantbclr
  2978)    call ExpDayNite(meantbclr_isccp,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2979) 
  2980)    ! (2d variables), loop over subcolumns to do expansion.
  2981)    do i=1,nscol_cosp
  2982)       tmp(1:Nday) = isccp%boxtau(1:Nday,i)      ! CAM version of boxtauisccp (time,column,profile)
  2983)       call ExpDayNite(tmp,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2984)       tau_isccp(1:ncol,i) = tmp(1:ncol)
  2985)       tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  2986)    end do
  2987) 
  2988)    do i=1,nscol_cosp
  2989)       tmp(1:Nday) = isccp%boxptop(1:Nday,i)     ! CAM version of boxtauisccp (time,column,profile)
  2990)       call ExpDayNite(tmp,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  2991)       cldptop_isccp(1:ncol,i) = tmp(1:ncol)
  2992)       tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  2993)    end do
  2994) 
  2995)    ! (3d variables), loop over tau and nprs_cosp/htmisr_cosp to do expansion.
  2996)    !!  I think there might be a problem here...
  2997)    do it=1,ntau_cosp
  2998)    do ip=1,nprs_cosp
  2999)       tmp(1:Nday) = isccp%fq_isccp(1:Nday,it,ip)
  3000)       call ExpDayNite(tmp,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)     
  3001)       clisccp2(1:ncol,it,ip) = tmp(1:ncol)      ! clisccp2 (time,tau,plev,profile)
  3002)       tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3003)    end do
  3004)    end do
  3005) 
  3006) 
  3007) end if
  3008) 
  3009) if (lmisr_sim) then
  3010)    do it=1,ntau_cosp
  3011)    do ihm=1,nhtmisr_cosp
  3012)       tmp(1:Nday) = misr%fq_MISR(1:Nday,it,ihm)
  3013)       call ExpDayNite(tmp,      Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)     
  3014)       clMISR(1:ncol,it,ihm) = tmp(1:ncol)                       ! clMISR (time,tau,CTH_height_bin,profile)
  3015)       tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3016)    end do
  3017)    end do
  3018) 
  3019)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  3020)    do i=1,ncol
  3021)         ! CAM clMISR (time,tau,CTH_height_bin,profile)
  3022)         do ihm=1,nhtmisr_cosp
  3023)         do it=1,ntau_cosp
  3024)            ihmt=(ihm-1)*ntau_cosp+it                    
  3025)            cld_misr(i,ihmt) = clMISR(i,it,ihm)                  ! cld_misr(pcols,nhtmisr_cosp*ntau_cosp)
  3026)         end do
  3027)         end do
  3028)    end do
  3029) end if
  3030) 
  3031) if (lfrac_out) then
  3032)    frac_out = sgx%frac_out                              ! frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  3033) 
  3034)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  3035)    ! CAM frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)  FIX
  3036)    do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  3037)    do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  3038)         ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                    
  3039)         scops_out(i,ihsc) = frac_out(i,isc,ihml)        ! scops_out(pcols,nht_cosp*nscol_cosp)
  3040)    end do
  3041)    end do
  3042) end if
  3043)  
  3044) if (lmodis_sim) then
  3045)       ! (1d variables from modis simulator)
  3046)       cltmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Fraction_Total_Mean
  3047)       call ExpDayNite(cltmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3048) 
  3049)       clwmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Fraction_Water_Mean
  3050)       call ExpDayNite(clwmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3051) 
  3052)       climodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Fraction_Ice_Mean
  3053)       call ExpDayNite(climodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3054) 
  3055)       clhmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Fraction_High_Mean
  3056)       call ExpDayNite(clhmodis,Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3057) 
  3058)       clmmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Fraction_Mid_Mean
  3059)       call ExpDayNite(clmmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3060) 
  3061)       cllmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Fraction_Low_Mean
  3062)       call ExpDayNite(cllmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3063) 
  3064)       tautmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_Total_Mean
  3065)       call ExpDayNite(tautmodis,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3066) 
  3067)       tauwmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_Water_Mean
  3068)       call ExpDayNite(tauwmodis,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3069) 
  3070)       tauimodis(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_Ice_Mean
  3071)       call ExpDayNite(tauimodis,        Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3072) 
  3073)       tautlogmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_Total_LogMean
  3074)       call ExpDayNite(tautlogmodis,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3075) 
  3076)       tauwlogmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_Water_LogMean
  3077)       call ExpDayNite(tauwlogmodis,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3078) 
  3079)       tauilogmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_Ice_LogMean
  3080)       call ExpDayNite(tauilogmodis,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3081) 
  3082)       reffclwmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Particle_Size_Water_Mean
  3083)       call ExpDayNite(reffclwmodis,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3084) 
  3085)       reffclimodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Particle_Size_Ice_Mean
  3086)       call ExpDayNite(reffclimodis,     Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3087) 
  3088)       pctmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Cloud_Top_Pressure_Total_Mean
  3089)       call ExpDayNite(pctmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3090) 
  3091)       lwpmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Liquid_Water_Path_Mean
  3092)       call ExpDayNite(lwpmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3093) 
  3094)       iwpmodis(1:Nday) = modis%Ice_Water_Path_Mean
  3095)       call ExpDayNite(iwpmodis, Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3096) 
  3097)       ! (3d variable), need to loop 
  3098)       do it=1,ntau_cosp_modis
  3099)       do ip=1,nprs_cosp
  3100)          tmp(1:Nday) = modis%Optical_Thickness_vs_Cloud_Top_Pressure(1:Nday,it,ip)
  3101)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)     
  3102)          clmodis(1:ncol,it,ip) = tmp(1:ncol)
  3103)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3104)       end do
  3105)       end do
  3106) 
  3107)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  3108)       do i=1,ncol
  3109)            ! CAM clmodis
  3110)            do ip=1,nprs_cosp
  3111)            do it=1,ntau_cosp_modis
  3112)               ipt=(ip-1)*ntau_cosp_modis+it
  3113)               clmodis_cam(i,ipt) = clmodis(i,it,ip)
  3114)            end do
  3115)            end do
  3116)       end do
  3117) end if
  3118) 
  3119)    !print *, 'Done mapping COSP output to local variables for running only ISCCP/MISR/MODIS on sunlit columns ...'
  3120) 
  3121) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3122) ! DEALLOCATE MEMORY for running only daylit columns
  3123) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3124)    call free_cosp_gridbox(gbx)
  3125)    call free_cosp_vgrid(vgrid)
  3126)    call free_cosp_subgrid(sgx)
  3127)    call free_cosp_sgradar(sgradar)
  3128)    call free_cosp_radarstats(stradar)
  3129)    call free_cosp_sglidar(sglidar)
  3130)    call free_cosp_lidarstats(stlidar)
  3131)    call free_cosp_isccp(isccp)
  3132)    call free_cosp_misr(misr) 
  3133)    call free_cosp_modis(modis)
  3134) 
  3135) end if !! if there are columns to run
  3136) 
  3137) end if  !!! END RUNNING COSP ONLY ON SUNLIT COLUMNS
  3138) 
  3139) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3140) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3141) !  RUN COSP FOR ONLY RADAR AND/OR LIDAR SIMULATORS (COSP SETUP/CALL #3)
  3142) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3143) !++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3144) 
  3145) if ((.not.cosp_runall) .and. (lradar_sim.or.llidar_sim)) then !! RUNNING RADAR/LIDAR  
  3146) 
  3147) ! Only run the lidar and radar simulators and their outputs
  3148) if (lradar_sim) then
  3149)    cfg%Lradar_sim= .true.
  3150)    cfg%Lcfaddbze94= .true.
  3151)    cfg%Ldbze94= .true.
  3152)    cfg%Lcltradar= .true.
  3153)    cfg%Lcltradar2= .true.
  3154)    cfg%Lclcalipso2= .true.
  3155)    cfg%Lcltlidarradar= .true.
  3156) end if
  3157) if (llidar_sim) then
  3158)    cfg%Llidar_sim= .true.
  3159)    cfg%Latb532= .true.
  3160)    cfg%LcfadLidarsr532= .true.
  3161)    cfg%Lclcalipso= .true.
  3162)    cfg%Lclhcalipso= .true.
  3163)    cfg%Lclisccp= .true.
  3164)    cfg%Lcllcalipso= .true.
  3165)    cfg%Lclmcalipso= .true.
  3166)    cfg%Lcltcalipso= .true.
  3167)    cfg%LparasolRefl= .true.
  3168)    cfg%LlidarBetaMol532= .true.
  3169) end if
  3170) 
  3171) ! Run cosp_stats.f90 for radar and lidar output
  3172) cfg%Lstats = .true.
  3173) 
  3174) ! Don't run the iscc/misr/modis or misr simulators by changing COSP input structure cfg
  3175) cfg%Lisccp_sim= .false.
  3176) cfg%Lmisr_sim= .false.
  3177) cfg%Lmodis_sim= .false.
  3178) 
  3179) ! Also set isccp,misr,modis output flags to false in COSP input structure cfg
  3180) cfg%Lalbisccp= .false.
  3181) cfg%Latb532= .false.
  3182) cfg%Lboxptopisccp= .false.
  3183) cfg%Lboxtauisccp= .false.
  3184) cfg%Lpctisccp= .false.
  3185) cfg%Ltauisccp= .false.
  3186) cfg%Lcltisccp= .false.
  3187) cfg%Lmeantbisccp= .false.
  3188) cfg%Lmeantbclrisccp= .false.
  3189) cfg%LclMISR= .false.
  3190) cfg%Lcltmodis= .false.
  3191) cfg%Lclwmodis= .false.
  3192) cfg%Lclimodis= .false.
  3193) cfg%Lclhmodis= .false.
  3194) cfg%Lclmmodis= .false.
  3195) cfg%Lcllmodis= .false.
  3196) cfg%Ltautmodis= .false.
  3197) cfg%Ltauwmodis= .false.
  3198) cfg%Ltauimodis= .false.
  3199) cfg%Ltautlogmodis= .false.
  3200) cfg%Ltauwlogmodis= .false.
  3201) cfg%Ltauilogmodis= .false.
  3202) cfg%Lreffclwmodis= .false.
  3203) cfg%Lreffclimodis= .false.
  3204) cfg%Lpctmodis= .false.
  3205) cfg%Llwpmodis= .false.
  3206) cfg%Liwpmodis= .false.
  3207) cfg%Lclmodis= .false.
  3208) 
  3209) ! Subsetting using an orbital curtain for radar and lidar simulators
  3210) ! Note: This is a very basic implementation and should be checked with other groups.
  3211) 
  3212) if (cosp_sample_atrain) then
  3213) 
  3214) ! Subsetting using the orbit data file.
  3215) ! Subsetting CAM columns that will have simulator run on them using time and geographic constraint
  3216) ! 1) time - use fractional calendar day (1-365), eliminates the need for time of day.
  3217) ! for day - CAM default is a NO_LEAP calendar
  3218) !    calendar = get_calendar()  !! 'NO_LEAP'
  3219) ! always use first 365 days of atrain orbit for 2008, even though 2008 has 366 days.
  3220) ! for time of day, use fractional value of calendar day.
  3221) ! note that you can use this to find exactly where the Atrain orbit has been during the CAM timestep
  3222)    !! OK, apply time constraint by using these values to find a beginning index to loop over
  3223)    !!! FIND WHERE THE ATRAIN HAS BEEN DURING THIS CAM TIMESTEP
  3224)    !!  This will enable you to loop over idxas,idxae instead of looping over 1, norbitdata
  3225)    !!! first time look through whole array using a plane old do loop, then
  3226)    !!! keep track of last time index to look for new time in the next time step
  3227)    !!! use information on time sequence in cloudsat orbit - map calendar day to index in big list
  3228)    !!! idxas will be private data stored at the module data level,  index of the last time match, it will be overwritten every time you call.
  3229)    !!idxas = beginning of cam timestep
  3230) ! 2) location - using lat/lon degree distance.
  3231) ! is it better to use a distance approach?  because of convergence at the poles, this will lead to un-uniform sampling
  3232) ! lat/lon only works for a rectangular grid.  what is the lat/lon threshold?  it will be resolution dependent!
  3233) !!! programming help notes
  3234) !! look in models/atm/cam/src/utils/time_manager.F90 for CAM time and date functions
  3235) !! get_curr_time used in models/atm/cam/src/control/cam_history.F90
  3236) !! for location - use lat_cosp, lon_cosp in the degrees_north and degrees_east already
  3237) 
  3238) !! initialize variable to decide if CAM column on A-train orbit
  3239)    atrain_use(1:ncol) = 0     !! array to indicate if column is in atrain orbit (1=yes,0=no)
  3240) 
  3241) !! TIME CONSTRAINT
  3242)    !! find idxas using calendar day from cam (calday) and from atrain (atrain_calday)
  3243)    cam_calday = get_curr_calday()    !returns fractional calendar day at end of current timestep
  3244)    atrain_calday = atrainday + (atrainhr*60*60.0_r8 + atrainmin*60.0_r8 + atrainsec)/86400.0_r8
  3245)    !!!print *, cam_calday
  3246)    !!!print *, atrain_calday(1:200)
  3247)     !! if first time through or after failed time search, start at the beginning of the file
  3248)    if (idxas .eq. 0) then
  3249)      idxas = 1
  3250)    end if
  3251) 
  3252)    !! loop to find idxas
  3253)    caldaydiff = abs(cam_calday - atrain_calday(idxas))
  3254)    caldaymindiff = caldaydiff
  3255)    caldaymatch = 0
  3256) 
  3257)    do while (caldaydiff .gt. atrain_daythresh)
  3258)       idxas = idxas + 1
  3259)       caldaydiff = abs(cam_calday - atrain_calday(idxas))
  3260)       if (caldaydiff .lt. atrain_daythresh) then
  3261)          !!print *, 'TIME MATCH FOUND ...'
  3262)          !!print *, cam_calday
  3263)          !!print *, atrain_calday(idxas)
  3264)          !!print *, caldaydiff
  3265)          caldaymatch = 1
  3266)       end if
  3267)       if (caldaydiff .lt. caldaymindiff) then
  3268)           caldaymindiff = caldaydiff
  3269)       end if
  3270) 
  3271)       if (idxas .ge. norbitdata) then
  3272)         !print *, 'No time match found for A-train orbit data, going back to beginning'
  3273)         idxas = 1
  3274)         caldaydiff = abs(cam_calday - atrain_calday(idxas))
  3275)         do while (caldaydiff .gt. atrain_daythresh)
  3276)            idxas = idxas + 1
  3277)            caldaydiff = abs(cam_calday - atrain_calday(idxas))
  3278)            if (caldaydiff .lt. atrain_daythresh) then
  3279)               !print *, 'TIME MATCH FOUND AFTER GOING BACK TO BEGINNING...'
  3280)               !print *, cam_calday
  3281)               !print *, atrain_calday(idxas)
  3282)               !print *, caldaydiff
  3283)               caldaymatch = 1
  3284)            end if
  3285)            if (caldaydiff .lt. caldaymindiff) then
  3286)                caldaymindiff = caldaydiff
  3287)            end if
  3288)            if (idxas .ge. norbitdata) then
  3289)              !print *, 'No time match found for A-train orbit data after search from beginning ERROR!'
  3290)              !print *, 'Need to increase atrain_daythresh for overpass. Min difference in days is:'
  3291)              !print *, caldaymindiff
  3292)              !! go back to the beginning for next time search
  3293)              idxas = 0
  3294)              !! exit the inner while
  3295)              exit
  3296)            end if
  3297)         end do
  3298)       end if
  3299)       !! no match found, exit the while
  3300)       if (idxas .eq. 0) then
  3301)         exit
  3302)       end if
  3303)    end do
  3304) 
  3305)    !! GEOGRAPHIC CONSTRAINT
  3306)    !! starting with a lat/lon degree criteria
  3307)    !! already have lat_cosp and lon_cosp in the right units.
  3308) 
  3309)    if (caldaymatch .eq. 1) then
  3310) 
  3311)       !! initialize 
  3312)       tmpvar(1:ntmp) = 0.0_r8
  3313)       tmpvar1(1:ntmp) = 0.0_r8
  3314)       tmpdiff(1:ntmp) = 0.0_r8
  3315)       idxlat(1:ntmp) = 0.0_r8
  3316)       idxlon(1:ntmp) = 0.0_r8
  3317)       idxsum(1:ntmp) = 0.0_r8
  3318) 
  3319)       !! test by forcing a location match
  3320)       !!!print *, atrainlat(idxas:idxas+10)
  3321)       !!!print *, atrainlon(idxas:idxas+10)
  3322)       !!lat_cosp(1)=atrainlat(idxas)
  3323)       !!lon_cosp(1)=atrainlon(idxas)
  3324) 
  3325)       do i = 1, ncol
  3326)           !! right latitude? atrainlat vs. lat_cosp(i)
  3327)           !! 1) create a vector of CAM latitude
  3328)           tmpvar(1:ntmp) = lat_cosp(i)
  3329)           !! 2) difference the CAM latitude with the Atrain orbit latitudes only over the right time!
  3330)           !! lehey compains "Two entities must be in shape conformance"
  3331)           tmpdiff = atrainlat(idxas:idxas+ntmp-1) - tmpvar
  3332)           !! 3) populate array to indicate if a matching latitude was found
  3333)           idxlat(1:ntmp) = 0
  3334)           do k = 1,ntmp
  3335)              if (abs(tmpdiff(k)) .lt. atrain_latthresh) then
  3336)                 !!!print *, 'LAT MATCH FOUND ...'
  3337)                 idxlat(k) = 1
  3338)              end if
  3339)           end do
  3340) 
  3341)           !! right longitude? atrainlon vs. lon_cosp(i) -- same thing as for latitude
  3342)           tmpvar(1:ntmp) = lon_cosp(i)
  3343) 
  3344)           !! convert atrainlon from -180:180 to 0:360 
  3345)           tmpvar1 = atrainlon(idxas:idxas+ntmp-1)
  3346)           do k = 1,ntmp
  3347)              if (tmpvar1(k) .lt. 0.0_r8) then
  3348)                 tmpvar1(k) = tmpvar1(k) + 360.0_r8
  3349)              end if
  3350)           end do
  3351)           !! difference atrainlon (tmpvar1) and camlon (tmpvar)
  3352)           tmpdiff = tmpvar1 - tmpvar
  3353)           idxlon(1:ntmp) = 0                     !! array to indicate if a matching longitude was found
  3354)           do k = 1,ntmp
  3355)              if (abs(tmpdiff(k)) .lt. atrain_lonthresh) then
  3356)                 !!!print *, 'LON MATCH FOUND ...'
  3357)                 idxlon(k) = 1
  3358)              end if
  3359)           end do
  3360) 
  3361)           !! sum the two query arrays and populate array to indicate if lat/lon criteria was met
  3362)           idxsum = idxlat + idxlon
  3363)           !!!print *, maxval(idxsum)
  3364)           if (maxval(idxsum) .eq. 2) then
  3365)              !!!print *, 'LOCATION AND CALDAY MATCH FOUND ...'
  3366)              !!atrain_use(i) = 1
  3367)           end if
  3368)       end do
  3369) 
  3370)    end if !! if calday match
  3371) 
  3372)    !!! assign indices for compression (note: code for day/nite from radsw.F90)
  3373)    Natrain = 0
  3374)    Nno = 0
  3375)    do i = 1, ncol
  3376)        !! figure out if part of atrain orbit and run_cosp criterion 
  3377)         if ((atrain_use(i) .eq. 1) .and. (run_cosp(i,lchnk))) then
  3378)            Natrain = Natrain + 1
  3379)            IdxAtrain(Natrain) = i
  3380)        else
  3381)            Nno = Nno + 1
  3382)            IdxNo(Nno) = i
  3383)        end if
  3384)     end do
  3385) 
  3386) else  !! not atrain sampling, 
  3387) 
  3388)     !!! assign indices for compression (note: code for day/nite from radsw.F90)
  3389)     Natrain = 0
  3390)     Nno = 0
  3391)     do i = 1, ncol
  3392)        !! figure out if columns meets run_cosp criterion 
  3393)         if (run_cosp(i,lchnk)) then
  3394)           Natrain = Natrain + 1
  3395)           IdxAtrain(Natrain) = i
  3396)        else
  3397)           Nno = Nno + 1
  3398)           IdxNo(Nno) = i
  3399)        end if
  3400)     end do
  3401) 
  3402) end if ! if atrain sampling
  3403) 
  3404) Npoints = Natrain
  3405) 
  3406) if (Natrain .lt. ncol) then  !! if a subset of columns are being run, do the below (i.e., only run it if you need to)
  3407) 
  3408) !!! rearrange input arrays - compress arrays so that COSP only runs on atrain columns
  3409) !e.g., a la
  3410) !   call CmpDayNite(E_pmid, pmid,       Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3411) ! (function from ..atm/cam/src/physics/cam/cmparray_mod.F90, see also radsw.F90)
  3412) !! CmpDayNite_2d_R_Copy(InArray, OutArray
  3413) 
  3414) call CmpDayNite(lon_cosp, lon_cosp_atrain,      Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3415) call CmpDayNite(lat_cosp, lat_cosp_atrain,      Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3416) call CmpDayNite(ptop, ptop_atrain,              Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3417) call CmpDayNite(state%pmid, pmid_atrain,         Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3418) call CmpDayNite(ztop, ztop_atrain,              Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3419) call CmpDayNite(zmid, zmid_atrain,              Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3420) call CmpDayNite(state%t,t_atrain,               Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3421) call CmpDayNite(rh, rh_atrain,                  Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3422) call CmpDayNite(q, q_atrain,                    Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3423) call CmpDayNite(concld, concld_atrain,          Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3424) call CmpDayNite(cld, cld_atrain,                Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3425) call CmpDayNite(state%ps, ps_atrain,            Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3426) call CmpDayNite(cam_in%ts ,ts_atrain,           Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3427) call CmpDayNite(landmask,landmask_atrain,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3428) call CmpDayNite(o3, o3_atrain,                  Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3429) call CmpDayNite(state%u(1:ncol,pver),us_atrain, Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, ncol)
  3430) call CmpDayNite(state%v(1:ncol,pver),vs_atrain, Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, ncol)
  3431) call CmpDayNite(mr_lsliq,mr_lsliq_atrain,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3432) call CmpDayNite(mr_lsice,mr_lsice_atrain,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3433) call CmpDayNite(mr_ccliq, mr_ccliq_atrain,      Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3434) call CmpDayNite(mr_ccice, mr_ccice_atrain,      Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3435) call CmpDayNite(rain_ls_interp, rain_ls_interp_atrain,          Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3436) call CmpDayNite(snow_ls_interp, snow_ls_interp_atrain,          Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3437) call CmpDayNite(grpl_ls_interp, grpl_ls_interp_atrain,          Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3438) call CmpDayNite(rain_cv_interp,rain_cv_interp_atrain,           Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3439) call CmpDayNite(snow_cv_interp,snow_cv_interp_atrain,           Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3440) call CmpDayNite(dtau_s,dtau_s_atrain,           Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3441) call CmpDayNite(dtau_c,dtau_c_atrain,           Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3442) call CmpDayNite(dtau_s_snow,dtau_s_snow_atrain,         Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3443) call CmpDayNite(dem_s,dem_s_atrain,             Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3444) call CmpDayNite(dem_c,dem_c_atrain,             Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3445) call CmpDayNite(dem_s_snow,dem_s_snow_atrain,           Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3446) 
  3447) !! need to loop over nhydro for reff_cosp_atrain
  3448) do i=1,nhydro
  3449)    call CmpDayNite(reff_cosp(:,:,i),tmp1,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pver)
  3450)    reff_cosp_atrain(:,:,i)=tmp1
  3451)    tmp1(1:pcols,1:pver)=R_UNDEF
  3452) end do
  3453) 
  3454) else  !! all columns used
  3455) 
  3456) !! running lidar or radar simulator on all columns
  3457) !! populate gbx inputs with all CAM columns
  3458)   lon_cosp_atrain=lon_cosp
  3459)   lat_cosp_atrain=lat_cosp
  3460)   ptop_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)           = ptop(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3461)   pmid_atrain=state%pmid
  3462)   ztop_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)           = ztop(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3463)   zmid_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)           = zmid(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3464)   t_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)              = state%t(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3465)   rh_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)             = rh(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3466)   q_atrain=q
  3467)   concld_atrain=concld
  3468)   cld_atrain=cld
  3469)   ps_atrain=state%ps
  3470)   ts_atrain=cam_in%ts
  3471)   landmask_atrain(1:ncol)              = landmask(1:ncol)
  3472)   o3_atrain=o3
  3473)   us_atrain(1:ncol)                    = state%u(1:ncol,pver)
  3474)   vs_atrain(1:ncol)                    = state%v(1:ncol,pver)
  3475)   mr_lsliq_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)       = mr_lsliq(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3476)   mr_lsice_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)       = mr_lsice(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3477)   mr_ccliq_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)       = mr_ccliq(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3478)   mr_ccice_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)       = mr_ccice(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3479)   rain_ls_interp_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver) = rain_ls_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3480)   snow_ls_interp_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver) = snow_ls_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3481)   grpl_ls_interp_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver) = grpl_ls_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3482)   rain_cv_interp_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver) = rain_cv_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3483)   snow_cv_interp_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver) = snow_cv_interp(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3484)   dtau_s_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)         = dtau_s(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3485)   dtau_c_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)         = dtau_c(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3486)   dtau_s_snow_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)    = dtau_s_snow(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3487)   dem_s_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)          = dem_s(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3488)   dem_c_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)          = dem_c(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3489)   dem_s_snow_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver)     = dem_s_snow(1:ncol,1:pver)
  3490)   reff_cosp_atrain(1:ncol,1:pver,:)    = reff_cosp(1:ncol,1:pver,:)
  3491) 
  3492) end if
  3493) 
  3494) 
  3495) !! if not atrain sampling and there are points that fit latlon criteria or there are points to sample within atrain
  3496) if (((.not.cosp_sample_atrain) .and. Natrain .gt. 0) .or. ((cosp_sample_atrain) .and. Natrain .gt. 0)) then
  3497) 
  3498) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3499) !  POPULATE COSP INPUT VARIABLE ("gbx") FROM CAM VARIABLES for atrain columns
  3500) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3501)    !print *, 'Allocating memory for gridbox type for atrain sub-columns only...'
  3502)    call construct_cosp_gridbox(time, &                          ! 1 double precision = real(r8) X
  3503)                                 time_bnds, &                    ! 1 double precision = real(r8)
  3504)                                 radar_freq, &                   ! 2 real(r8) X
  3505)                                 surface_radar, &                ! 3 integer X
  3506)                                 use_mie_tables, &               ! 4 integer X
  3507)                                 use_gas_abs, &                  ! 5 integer X
  3508)                                 do_ray, &                       ! 6 integer X 
  3509)                                 melt_lay, &                     ! 7 integer X 
  3510)                                 k2, &                           ! 8 real(r8) X
  3511)                                 Npoints, &                      ! 9 integer X
  3512)                                 Nlevels, &                      ! 10 integer X
  3513)                                 ncolumns,&                      ! 11 integer X
  3514)                                 nhydro,&                        ! 12 integer X
  3515)                                 Nprmts_max_hydro,&              ! 13 integer X
  3516)                                 Naero,&                         ! 14 integer X
  3517)                                 Nprmts_max_aero,&               ! 15 integer X
  3518)                                 Npoints_it, &                   ! 16 integer X
  3519)                                 lidar_ice_type,&                ! 17 integer X
  3520)                                 isccp_topheight,&               ! 18 integer X
  3521)                                 isccp_topheight_direction,&     ! 19 integer X
  3522)                                 overlap,&                       ! 20 integer X
  3523)                                 emsfc_lw, &                     ! 21 real X
  3524)                                 use_precipitation_fluxes,&      ! 22 logical X
  3525)                                 use_reff, &                     ! 23 logical X
  3526)                                 Platform, &                     ! 24 integer X
  3527)                                 Satellite, &                    ! 25 integer X
  3528)                                 Instrument, &                   ! 26 integer X
  3529)                                 Nchannels, &                    ! 27 integer X
  3530)                                 ZenAng, &                       ! 28 real(r8) X
  3531)                                 Channels(1:Nchannels),&         ! 29 integer X
  3532)                                 Surfem(1:Nchannels),&           ! 30 real(r8) X
  3533)                                 co2(1,1),&                      ! 31 real(r8) X
  3534)                                 ch4(1,1),&                      ! 32 real(r8) X
  3535)                                 n2o(1,1),&                      ! 33 real(r8) X
  3536)                                 co,&                            ! 34 real(r8) X
  3537)                                 gbx)                            ! OUT
  3538)     
  3539)    !print *, 'Populating input structure for COSP for running lidar/radar simulators only...'
  3540)    !! be very explicit about gbx structure sizes.
  3541)    !! flip vertical dimension from COSP convention to CAM convention
  3542)    !! Npoints can be ncol or Natrain - so here I just specify dimensions as Npoints
  3543)    gbx%longitude = lon_cosp_atrain(1:Npoints)                   ! lon (degrees_east)
  3544)    gbx%latitude = lat_cosp_atrain(1:Npoints)                    ! lat (degrees_north)
  3545)    gbx%p = ptop_atrain(1:Npoints,1:pver)                        ! p_in_full_levels (Pa),upper interface (flipping done above)
  3546)    gbx%ph = pmid_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)                    ! p_in_half_levels (Pa)
  3547)    gbx%zlev = ztop_atrain(1:Npoints,1:pver)                     ! height_in_full_levels (m),upper interface,asl (flipping done above)
  3548)    gbx%zlev_half = zmid_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)             ! height_in_half_levels (m),asl
  3549)    gbx%T = t_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)                        ! air_temperature (K)
  3550)    gbx%q = rh_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)                       ! relative humidity wrt water 
  3551)                                                                 ! note: it is confusing that it is called "q" within cosp,
  3552)                                                                 ! but it is rh according to Yuying
  3553)    gbx%sh = q_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)                       ! specific humidity (kg/kg), range [0,0.019ish]
  3554)    gbx%cca = concld_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)                 ! convective_cloud_amount (0-1)
  3555)    gbx%tca = cld_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)                    ! total_cloud_amount (0-1)
  3556)    gbx%psfc = ps_atrain(1:Npoints)                              ! surface pressure (Pa)
  3557)    gbx%skt  = ts_atrain(1:Npoints)                              ! skin temperature (K)
  3558)    gbx%land = landmask_atrain(1:Npoints)                        ! landmask (0 or 1)
  3559)    gbx%mr_ozone  = o3_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)               ! ozone mass mixing ratio (kg/kg)
  3560)    gbx%u_wind  = us_atrain(1:Npoints)                           ! surface u_wind (m/s)
  3561)    gbx%v_wind  = vs_atrain(1:Npoints)                           ! surface v_wind (m/s)
  3562)    gbx%sunlit  = 1
  3563)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_LSCLIQ) = mr_lsliq_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)    ! mr_lsliq, mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)
  3564)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_LSCICE) = mr_lsice_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)    ! mr_lsice - mixing_ratio_large_scale_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  3565)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_CVCLIQ) = mr_ccliq_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)    ! mr_ccliq - mixing_ratio_convective_cloud_liquid (kg/kg)
  3566)    gbx%mr_hydro(:,:,I_CVCICE) = mr_ccice_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)    ! mr_ccice - mixing_ratio_convective_cloud_ice (kg/kg)
  3567)    gbx%rain_ls = rain_ls_interp_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)             ! midpoint gbm
  3568)    gbx%snow_ls = snow_ls_interp_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)             ! midpoint gbm                  
  3569)    gbx%grpl_ls = grpl_ls_interp_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)             ! midpoint gbm
  3570)    gbx%rain_cv = rain_cv_interp_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)             ! midpoint gbm
  3571)    gbx%snow_cv = snow_cv_interp_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)             ! midpoint gbm
  3572)    gbx%Reff = reff_cosp_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1,:)
  3573)    gbx%dtau_s   = dtau_s_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)
  3574)    gbx%dtau_c   = dtau_c_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)
  3575)    gbx%dtau_s_snow   = dtau_s_snow_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)
  3576)    gbx%dem_s    = dem_s_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)
  3577)    gbx%dem_c    = dem_c_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)
  3578)    gbx%dem_s_snow    = dem_s_snow_atrain(1:Npoints,pver:1:-1)
  3579) 
  3580) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3581) ! STARTUP RELATED TO COSP OUTPUT (see cosp.F90) for atrain columns
  3582) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3583) ! Note: COSP output variables are sgx (sub-grid outputs), sgradar (radar outputs), sglidar (lidar outputs), 
  3584) ! isccp (isccp outputs), misr (misr simulator outputs), vgrid (vertical grid info), stradar 
  3585) ! (summary statistics radar simulator), stlidar (summary statistics lidar simulator)
  3586) 
  3587) ! Define new vertical grid
  3588)    !print *, 'Defining new vertical grid...'
  3589)    call construct_cosp_vgrid(gbx,nlr,use_vgrid,csat_vgrid,vgrid)
  3590)         
  3591) ! Allocate memory for output
  3592)    !print *, 'Allocating memory for other types...'
  3593)    call construct_cosp_subgrid(Npoints, ncolumns, Nlevels, sgx)
  3594)    call construct_cosp_sgradar(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,nhydro,sgradar)
  3595)    call construct_cosp_radarstats(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,vgrid%Nlvgrid,nhydro,stradar)
  3596)    call construct_cosp_sglidar(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,nhydro,PARASOL_NREFL,sglidar)
  3597)    call construct_cosp_lidarstats(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,vgrid%Nlvgrid,nhydro,PARASOL_NREFL,stlidar)
  3598)    call construct_cosp_isccp(cfg,Npoints,ncolumns,Nlevels,isccp)
  3599)    call construct_cosp_misr(cfg,Npoints,misr)
  3600)    !! new for cosp v1.3
  3601)    call construct_cosp_modis(cfg,Npoints,modis)
  3602) 
  3603) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3604) !  RUN COSP - RADAR/LIDAR only
  3605) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3606) 
  3607)    !print *, 'Calling the COSP simulator and running on all/atrain columns...'
  3608)    call cosp(overlap,ncolumns,cfg,vgrid,gbx,sgx,sgradar,sglidar,isccp,misr,modis,stradar,stlidar)
  3609) 
  3610) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3611) !  TRANSLATE COSP OUTPUT INTO INDIVIDUAL VARIABLES FOR OUTPUT (see nc_write_cosp_1d in cosp_io.f90)
  3612) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3613) 
  3614)    ! Map from COSP output to CAM output, only for simulators that were run!
  3615)    ! Populate CAM vars with COSP output (the reasoning for this is based on cosp_io.f90)
  3616)    !! steps 1) set as fill value, 2) fill in the columns calculated by COSP, 3) expand array
  3617)    ! Note: To expand to output CAM arrays, use ExpDayNite (function from ..atm/cam/src/physics/cam/cmparray_mod.F90, see also radsw.F90)
  3618)    ! e.g.,    call ExpDayNite(solin,    Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3619)    !   call ExpDayNite(pmxrgn,  Nday, IdxDay, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols, 1, pverp)
  3620) 
  3621) if (lradar_sim) then
  3622) 
  3623)    if (Natrain .lt. ncol) then  
  3624)       ! (1d variables from radar simulator)
  3625)       cldtot_calcs(1:Natrain)=stradar%radar_lidar_tcc   ! CAM version of cltlidarradar (time,profile)
  3626)       call ExpDayNite(cldtot_calcs,     Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3627)       cldtot_cs(1:Natrain)=stradar%radar_tcc    ! CAM version of cltradar (time,profile)
  3628)       call ExpDayNite(cldtot_cs,        Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3629)       cldtot_cs2(1:Natrain)=stradar%radar_tcc_2 ! CAM version of cltradar2 (time,profile)
  3630)       call ExpDayNite(cldtot_cs2,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3631) 
  3632) 
  3633)       ! (2d variables from radar simulator), loop over nht_cosp to do expansion.
  3634)       do i=1,nht_cosp
  3635)          tmp(1:Natrain) = stradar%lidar_only_freq_cloud(1:Natrain,i)    ! CAM version of clcalipso2 (time,height,profile)
  3636)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3637)          cld_cal_notcs(1:ncol,i)=tmp(1:ncol)
  3638)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3639)       end do
  3640) 
  3641)       ! (3d variables from radar simulator), loop over tau and plev to do expansion.
  3642)       do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  3643)       do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  3644)          tmp(1:Natrain) = sgradar%Ze_tot(1:Natrain,isc,ihml)
  3645)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)       
  3646)          dbze94(1:ncol,isc,ihml)=tmp(1:ncol)            ! dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)      
  3647)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF   
  3648)       end do
  3649)       end do
  3650)       do id=1,ndbze_cosp
  3651)       do ih=1,nht_cosp
  3652)          tmp(1:Natrain) = stradar%cfad_ze(1:Natrain,id,ih)
  3653)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)       
  3654)          cfad_dbze94(1:ncol,id,ih)=tmp(1:ncol)          ! cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile)
  3655)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF                   
  3656)       end do
  3657)       end do
  3658) 
  3659)    else
  3660)       ! (1d variables)
  3661)       cldtot_calcs(1:ncol) = stradar%radar_lidar_tcc            ! CAM version of cltlidarradar (time,profile)
  3662)       cldtot_cs(1:ncol)=stradar%radar_tcc
  3663)       cldtot_cs2(1:ncol)=stradar%radar_tcc_2
  3664)       ! (2d variables)
  3665)       cld_cal_notcs(1:ncol,1:nht_cosp) = stradar%lidar_only_freq_cloud  ! CAM version of clcalipso2 (time,height,profile)
  3666)       ! (3d variables)
  3667)       dbze94(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp) = sgradar%Ze_tot  ! dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  3668)       cfad_dbze94(1:ncol,1:ndbze_cosp,1:nht_cosp) = stradar%cfad_ze     ! cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile)
  3669)    end if
  3670) 
  3671)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  3672)    do i=1,ncol
  3673)         ! CAM dbze94 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  3674)         do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  3675)         do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  3676)            ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                 
  3677)            dbze_cs(i,ihsc) = dbze94(i,isc,ihml)                 ! dbze_cs(pcols,pver*nscol_cosp) 
  3678)         end do
  3679)         end do
  3680)         ! CAM cfad_dbze94 (time,height,dbze,profile) 
  3681)         do ih=1,nht_cosp
  3682)         do id=1,ndbze_cosp
  3683)            ihd=(ih-1)*ndbze_cosp+id                     
  3684)            cfad_dbze94_cs(i,ihd) = cfad_dbze94(i,id,ih)         ! cfad_dbze94_cs(pcols,nht_cosp*ndbze_cosp)
  3685)         end do
  3686)         end do
  3687)    end do
  3688) 
  3689) end if
  3690) 
  3691) if (llidar_sim) then
  3692) 
  3693)    if (Natrain .lt. ncol) then 
  3694)       ! (1d variables from lidar simulator)
  3695)       cldlow_cal(1:Natrain) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,1)     ! CAM version of cllcalipso (time,profile)
  3696)       call ExpDayNite(cldlow_cal,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3697)       cldmed_cal(1:Natrain) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,2)     ! CAM version of clmcalipso (time,profile)
  3698)       call ExpDayNite(cldmed_cal,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3699)       cldhgh_cal(1:Natrain) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,3)     ! CAM version of clhcalipso (time,profile)
  3700)       call ExpDayNite(cldhgh_cal,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3701)       cldtot_cal(1:Natrain) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,4)     ! CAM version of cltcalipso (time,profile)
  3702)       call ExpDayNite(cldtot_cal,       Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3703) 
  3704)       ! (2d variables from lidar simulator), loop over 2nd dimension to do expansion.
  3705)       do i=1,nht_cosp
  3706)          tmp(1:Natrain) = stlidar%lidarcld(1:Natrain,i) ! CAM version of clcalipso (time,height,profile)
  3707)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3708)          cld_cal(1:ncol,i) = tmp(1:ncol)
  3709)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3710)       end do
  3711) 
  3712)       do i=1,nhtml_cosp
  3713)          tmp(1:Natrain) = sglidar%beta_mol(1:Natrain,i) ! CAM version of beta_mol532 (time,height_mlev,profile) 
  3714)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3715)          mol532_cal(1:ncol,i) = tmp(1:ncol)
  3716)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3717)       end do
  3718) 
  3719)       do i=1,nsza_cosp
  3720)          tmp(1:Natrain) = stlidar%parasolrefl(1:Natrain,i)      ! CAM version of parasolrefl (time,sza,profile)
  3721)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)
  3722)          refl_parasol(1:ncol,i) = tmp(1:ncol)
  3723)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF
  3724)       end do
  3725) 
  3726)       ! (3d variables from lidar simulator), loop over 2nd and 3rd dimensions to do expansion.
  3727)       do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  3728)       do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  3729)          tmp(1:Natrain) = sglidar%beta_tot(1:Natrain,isc,ihml)
  3730)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)       
  3731)          atb532(1:ncol,isc,ihml) = tmp(1:ncol)          ! atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  3732)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF   
  3733)       end do
  3734)       end do
  3735) 
  3736)       do is=1,nsr_cosp
  3737)       do ih=1,nht_cosp
  3738)          tmp(1:Natrain) = stlidar%cfad_sr(1:Natrain,is,ih)      
  3739)          call ExpDayNite(tmp,   Natrain, IdxAtrain, Nno, IdxNo, 1, pcols)       
  3740)          cfad_lidarsr532(1:ncol,is,ih) = tmp(1:ncol)    ! cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  3741)          tmp(1:pcols)=R_UNDEF           
  3742)       end do
  3743)       end do
  3744) 
  3745)    else
  3746)       ! (1d variables)
  3747)       cldlow_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,1)                ! CAM version of cllcalipso (time,profile)      
  3748)       cldmed_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,2)                ! CAM version of clmcalipso (time,profile)
  3749)       cldhgh_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,3)                ! CAM version of clhcalipso (time,profile)
  3750)       cldtot_cal(1:ncol) = stlidar%cldlayer(:,4)                ! CAM version of cltcalipso (time,profile)
  3751)       ! (2d variables)
  3752)       cld_cal(1:ncol,1:nht_cosp) = stlidar%lidarcld             ! CAM version of clcalipso (time,height,profile)
  3753)       mol532_cal(1:ncol,1:nhtml_cosp) = sglidar%beta_mol        ! CAM version of beta_mol532 (time,height_mlev,profile)
  3754)       refl_parasol(1:ncol,1:nsza_cosp) = stlidar%parasolrefl    ! CAM version of parasolrefl (time,sza,profile)
  3755)       ! (3d variables)
  3756)       atb532(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp) = sglidar%beta_tot       ! atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  3757)       cfad_lidarsr532(1:ncol,1:nsr_cosp,1:nht_cosp)= stlidar%cfad_sr    ! cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  3758)    end if
  3759) 
  3760)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  3761)    do i=1,ncol
  3762)         ! CAM atb532 (time,height_mlev,column,profile)  FIX
  3763)         do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  3764)         do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  3765)            ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                 
  3766)            atb532_cal(i,ihsc) = atb532(i,isc,ihml)              ! atb532_cal(pcols,nht_cosp*nscol_cosp)
  3767)         end do
  3768)         end do
  3769)         ! CAM cfad_lidarsr532 (time,height,scat_ratio,profile)
  3770)         do ih=1,nht_cosp
  3771)         do is=1,nsr_cosp
  3772)            ihs=(ih-1)*nsr_cosp+is                       
  3773)            cfad_sr532_cal(i,ihs) = cfad_lidarsr532(i,is,ih)  ! cfad_sr532_cal(pcols,nht_cosp*nsr_cosp)
  3774)         end do
  3775)         end do
  3776)    end do
  3777) 
  3778) end if
  3779) 
  3780) if ((lfrac_out) .and. (.not.lradar_sim) .and. (.not.llidar_sim)) then
  3781)    frac_out(1:ncol,1:nscol_cosp,1:nhtml_cosp) = sgx%frac_out            ! frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)
  3782) 
  3783)    ! Use high-dimensional output to populate CAM collapsed output variables
  3784)    ! CAM frac_out (time,height_mlev,column,profile)  FIX
  3785)    do ihml=1,nhtml_cosp
  3786)    do isc=1,nscol_cosp
  3787)         ihsc=(ihml-1)*nscol_cosp+isc                    
  3788)         scops_out(i,ihsc) = frac_out(i,isc,ihml)        ! scops_out(pcols,nht_cosp*nscol_cosp)
  3789)    end do
  3790)    end do
  3791) end if
  3792) 
  3793)    !print *, 'Done mapping COSP output to local variables for running only radar/lidar ...'
  3794) 
  3795) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3796) ! DEALLOCATE MEMORY for running only radar/lidar
  3797) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3798)    call free_cosp_gridbox(gbx)
  3799)    call free_cosp_vgrid(vgrid)
  3800)    call free_cosp_subgrid(sgx)
  3801)    call free_cosp_sgradar(sgradar)
  3802)    call free_cosp_radarstats(stradar)
  3803)    call free_cosp_sglidar(sglidar)
  3804)    call free_cosp_lidarstats(stlidar)
  3805)    call free_cosp_isccp(isccp)
  3806)    call free_cosp_misr(misr) 
  3807)    call free_cosp_modis(modis)
  3808) 
  3809) end if !! end if there are atrain columns to run
  3810) 
  3811) end if  !!! END RUNNING COSP ONLY RADAR/LIDAR
  3812) 
  3813) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3814) ! OUTFLD CALLS
  3815) !+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++
  3816) 
  3817) !!! ISCCP OUTPUTS
  3818)    if (lisccp_sim) then
  3819)       call outfld('FISCCP1_COSP',clisccp2, pcols,lchnk)
  3820)       call outfld('CLDTOT_ISCCP',cldtot_isccp    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3821)       !! weight meancldalb_isccp by the cloud fraction
  3822)       !! where there is no isccp cloud fraction, set meancldalb_isccp = R_UNDEF
  3823)       !! weight meanptop_isccp  by the cloud fraction
  3824)       !! where there is no isccp cloud fraction, set meanptop_isccp = R_UNDEF
  3825)       !! weight meantau_isccp by the cloud fraction
  3826)       !! where there is no isccp cloud fraction, set meantau_isccp = R_UNDEF
  3827)       where (cldtot_isccp(:ncol) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  3828)          meancldalb_isccp(:ncol) = R_UNDEF
  3829)          meanptop_isccp(:ncol) = R_UNDEF
  3830)          meantau_isccp(:ncol) = R_UNDEF
  3831)       elsewhere
  3832)          meancldalb_isccp(:ncol) = meancldalb_isccp(:ncol)*cldtot_isccp(:ncol)
  3833)          meanptop_isccp(:ncol) = meanptop_isccp(:ncol)*cldtot_isccp(:ncol)
  3834)          meantau_isccp(:ncol) = meantau_isccp(:ncol)*cldtot_isccp(:ncol)
  3835)       end where      
  3836)       call outfld('MEANCLDALB_ISCCP',meancldalb_isccp,pcols,lchnk)
  3837)       call outfld('MEANPTOP_ISCCP',meanptop_isccp    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3838)       call outfld('MEANTAU_ISCCP',meantau_isccp  ,pcols,lchnk)
  3839)       call outfld('MEANTB_ISCCP',     meantb_isccp   ,pcols,lchnk)
  3840)       call outfld('MEANTBCLR_ISCCP',  meantbclr_isccp ,pcols,lchnk)
  3841)    end if
  3842) 
  3843) !!! LIDAR SIMULATOR OUTPUTS
  3844)    if (llidar_sim) then
  3845)       call outfld('CLDLOW_CAL',cldlow_cal    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3846)       call outfld('CLDMED_CAL',cldmed_cal    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3847)       call outfld('CLDHGH_CAL',cldhgh_cal    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3848)       call outfld('CLDTOT_CAL',cldtot_cal    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3849) 
  3850)       where (cld_cal(:ncol,:nht_cosp) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  3851)             !! setting missing values to 0 (clear air).  
  3852)             !! I'm not sure why COSP produces a mix of R_UNDEF and realvalue in the nht_cosp dimension.
  3853)             cld_cal(:ncol,:nht_cosp) = 0.0_r8
  3854)       end where  
  3855)       call outfld('CLD_CAL',cld_cal    ,pcols,lchnk)  !! fails check_accum if 'A'
  3856)       call outfld('MOL532_CAL',mol532_cal    ,pcols,lchnk)
  3857) 
  3858)       where (cfad_sr532_cal(:ncol,:nht_cosp*nsr_cosp) .eq. R_UNDEF)
  3859) !! fails check_accum if this is set... with ht_cosp set relative to sea level, mix of R_UNDEF and realvalue
  3860) !!            cfad_sr532_cal(:ncol,:nht_cosp*nsr_cosp) = R_UNDEF
  3861)             cfad_sr532_cal(:ncol,:nht_cosp*nsr_cosp) = 0.0_r8
